I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
Web roadmap derives milestone status from slice heuristics instead of authoritative GSD milestone state
## Summary

The web Roadmap view derives milestone status from slice completion heuristics instead of using the authoritative milestone status from GSD state. This causes incorrect status rendering for milestones whose lifecycle state and validation verdict differ.

## Problem

In the current web UI:

- `web/components/gsd/roadmap.tsx` calls `getMilestoneStatus()` from `web/lib/workspace-status.ts`
- `getMilestoneStatus()` infers milestone state using only:
  - whether all slices are done
  - whether the milestone is the active milestone
  - whether any slice is done

Current logic:

```ts
export function getMilestoneStatus(milestone, active) {
  if (milestone.slices.length > 0 && milestone.slices.every((slice) => slice.done)) {
    return "done"
  }
  if (active.milestoneId === milestone.id) {
    return "in-progress"
  }
  return milestone.slices.some((slice) => slice.done) ? "in-progress" : "pending"
}
```

This is not aligned with GSD's actual milestone model.

## Why this is wrong

GSD milestone state has milestone-level semantics that are separate from slice completion:

- lifecycle status: `complete` / `active` / `pending` / `parked`
- validation verdict: `pass` / `needs-attention` / `needs-remediation`

The roadmap page currently does not consume milestone-level status at all. Instead, it reconstructs a UI state from slice progress.

That means milestones can render incorrectly when:

- the milestone is complete but validation is `needs-attention`
- the milestone has summary / validation artifacts that represent a terminal state
- milestone state and slice completion are not perfectly representable by the three inferred UI buckets

## Root cause

The web workspace index does not expose milestone-level status.

`src/resources/extensions/gsd/workspace-index.ts` currently returns milestone entries shaped roughly like:

```ts
{
  id,
  title,
  roadmapPath,
  slices,
}
```

It does **not** include:

- authoritative milestone status
- validation verdict
- summary existence / terminal milestone information

So the roadmap UI has no choice except to guess.

## Expected behavior

The Roadmap view should render milestone status from authoritative milestone state, not from slice heuristics.

At minimum, it should consume milestone lifecycle status from the engine/index layer.

Ideally, the UI contract should include both:

- `status: complete | active | pending | parked`
- `validationVerdict?: pass | needs-attention | needs-remediation`

## Suggested fix

### Option A (preferred)
Extend `WorkspaceMilestoneTarget` in `src/resources/extensions/gsd/workspace-index.ts` and `web/lib/gsd-workspace-store.tsx` to include milestone-level state:

```ts
interface WorkspaceMilestoneTarget {
  id: string
  title: string
  roadmapPath?: string
  status: "complete" | "active" | "pending" | "parked"
  validationVerdict?: "pass" | "needs-attention" | "needs-remediation"
  slices: WorkspaceSliceTarget[]
}
```

Populate `status` from `deriveState(basePath).registry`, and populate `validationVerdict` from milestone validation data.

Then update `web/components/gsd/roadmap.tsx` to render from those fields directly.

### Option B (partial)
If you want a smaller first step, at least add milestone `status` to the workspace index and make `getMilestoneStatus()` prefer that value before falling back to the current heuristic.

## Relevant files

- `web/components/gsd/roadmap.tsx`
- `web/lib/workspace-status.ts`
- `src/resources/extensions/gsd/workspace-index.ts`
- `web/lib/gsd-workspace-store.tsx`
- `src/resources/extensions/gsd/state.ts` (authoritative state source)
- `src/resources/extensions/gsd/visualizer-data.ts` / `web/lib/visualizer-types.ts` (already carry milestone-level status in another path)

## Impact

This makes the Roadmap view disagree with the actual GSD state model and can mislead users about milestone progress/completion semantics.

In practice, milestones with different validation outcomes can appear indistinguishable or be rendered with the wrong status emphasis in the Roadmap page.


</pr_description>

     3	  WorkspaceSliceTarget,
     4	  WorkspaceTaskTarget,
     5	} from "./gsd-workspace-store"
     6	
     7	export type ItemStatus = "done" | "in-progress" | "pending"
     8	
     9	export function getMilestoneStatus(
    10	  milestone: WorkspaceMilestoneTarget,
    11	  active: { milestoneId?: string },
    12	): ItemStatus {
    13	  if (milestone.slices.length > 0 && milestone.slices.every((slice) => slice.done)) {
    14	    return "done"
    15	  }
    16	  if (active.milestoneId === milestone.id) {
    17	    return "in-progress"
    18	  }
    19	  return milestone.slices.some((slice) => slice.done) ? "in-progress" : "pending"
    20	}
    21	
    22	export function getSliceStatus(
    23	  milestoneId: string,
    24	  slice: WorkspaceSliceTarget,
    25	  active: { milestoneId?: string; sliceId?: string },
    26	): ItemStatus {
    27	  if (slice.done) return "done"
    28	  if (active.milestoneId === milestoneId && active.sliceId === slice.id) return "in-progress"
    29	  return "pending"
    30	}
    31	
    32	export function getTaskStatus(
    33	  milestoneId: string,
    34	  sliceId: string,

   405	// Discriminated union for extension UI requests — matches the authoritative
   406	// RpcExtensionUIRequest from rpc-types.ts. Blocking methods queue in pendingUiRequests;
   407	// fire-and-forget methods update state maps directly.
   408	export type ExtensionUiRequestEvent =
   409	  | { type: "extension_ui_request"; id: string; method: "select"; title: string; options: string[]; timeout?: number; allowMultiple?: boolean }
   410	  | { type: "extension_ui_request"; id: string; method: "confirm"; title: string; message: string; timeout?: number }
   411	  | { type: "extension_ui_request"; id: string; method: "input"; title: string; placeholder?: string; timeout?: number }
   412	  | { type: "extension_ui_request"; id: string; method: "editor"; title: string; prefill?: string }
   413	  | { type: "extension_ui_request"; id: string; method: "notify"; message: string; notifyType?: "info" | "warning" | "error" }
   414	  | { type: "extension_ui_request"; id: string; method: "setStatus"; statusKey: string; statusText: string | undefined }
   415	  | { type: "extension_ui_request"; id: string; method: "setWidget"; widgetKey: string; widgetLines: string[] | undefined; widgetPlacement?: "aboveEditor" | "belowEditor" }
   416	  | { type: "extension_ui_request"; id: string; method: "setTitle"; title: string }
   417	  | { type: "extension_ui_request"; id: string; method: "set_editor_text"; text: string }

   461	export type WorkspaceEvent =
   462	  | BridgeStatusEvent
   463	  | LiveStateInvalidationEvent
   464	  | ExtensionUiRequestEvent
   465	  | ExtensionErrorEvent
   466	  | MessageUpdateEvent
   467	  | ToolExecutionStartEvent
   468	  | ToolExecutionEndEvent
   469	  | AgentEndEvent
   470	  | TurnEndEvent
   471	  | ({ type: Exclude<string, "bridge_status" | "live_state_invalidation" | "extension_ui_request" | "extension_error" | "message_update" | "tool_execution_start" | "tool_execution_end" | "agent_end" | "turn_end">; [key: string]: unknown } & Record<string, unknown>)
   472	
   473	export function isWorkspaceEvent(value: unknown): value is WorkspaceEvent {
   474	  return value !== null && typeof value === "object" && typeof (value as Record<string, unknown>).type === "string"
   475	}

    66	// Extract milestone title from roadmap header without using parsers.
    67	// Falls back to the milestone ID if no title line found.
    68	function titleFromRoadmapHeader(content: string, fallbackId: string): string {
    69	  // Parse the "# M001: Title" header directly
    70	  const match = content.match(/^#\s+M\d+(?:-[a-z0-9]{6})?[^:]*:\s*(.+)/m);
    71	  return match?.[1]?.trim() || fallbackId;
    72	}
    73	
    74	async function indexSlice(basePath: string, milestoneId: string, sliceId: string, fallbackTitle: string, done: boolean, roadmapMeta?: { risk?: RiskLevel; depends?: string[]; demo?: string }): Promise<WorkspaceSliceTarget> {
    75	  const planPath = resolveSliceFile(basePath, milestoneId, sliceId, "PLAN") ?? undefined;
    76	  const summaryPath = resolveSliceFile(basePath, milestoneId, sliceId, "SUMMARY") ?? undefined;
    77	  const uatPath = resolveSliceFile(basePath, milestoneId, sliceId, "UAT") ?? undefined;
    78	  const tasksDir = resolveTasksDir(basePath, milestoneId, sliceId) ?? undefined;
    79	
    80	  const tasks: WorkspaceTaskTarget[] = [];
    81	  let title = fallbackTitle;
    82	
    83	  // Prefer DB for task data, fall back to file parsing when DB has no data
    84	  let usedDb = false;
    85	  if (isDbAvailable()) {
    86	    const dbTasks = getSliceTasks(milestoneId, sliceId);
    87	    if (dbTasks.length > 0) {
    88	      usedDb = true;
    89	      for (const task of dbTasks) {
    90	        title = fallbackTitle; // title comes from slice-level data, not plan
    91	        tasks.push({
    92	          id: task.id,
    93	          title: task.title,
    94	          done: task.status === "complete" || task.status === "done",
    95	          planPath: resolveTaskFile(basePath, milestoneId, sliceId, task.id, "PLAN") ?? undefined,
    96	          summaryPath: resolveTaskFile(basePath, milestoneId, sliceId, task.id, "SUMMARY") ?? undefined,
    97	        });
    98	      }
    99	    }
   100	  }
   101	  if (!usedDb && planPath) {
   102	    // File-based fallback: parse slice plan for task entries
   103	    const planContent = await loadFile(planPath);
   104	    if (planContent) {
   105	      const parsed = parsePlan(planContent);
   106	      for (const task of parsed.tasks) {
   107	        tasks.push({
   108	          id: task.id,
   109	          title: task.title,
   110	          done: task.done,
   111	          planPath: resolveTaskFile(basePath, milestoneId, sliceId, task.id, "PLAN") ?? undefined,
   112	          summaryPath: resolveTaskFile(basePath, milestoneId, sliceId, task.id, "SUMMARY") ?? undefined,
   113	        });
   114	      }
   115	    }
   116	  }
   117	
   118	  return {
   119	    id: sliceId,
   120	    title,
   121	    done,
   122	    planPath,
   123	    summaryPath,
   124	    uatPath,
   125	    tasksDir,
   126	    branch: getSliceBranchName(milestoneId, sliceId, detectWorktreeName(basePath)),
   127	    risk: roadmapMeta?.risk,
   128	    depends: roadmapMeta?.depends,
   129	    demo: roadmapMeta?.demo,
   130	    tasks,
   131	  };
   132	}
   133	
   134	export interface IndexWorkspaceOptions {
   135	  validate?: boolean;
   136	}
   137	
   138	export async function indexWorkspace(basePath: string, opts: IndexWorkspaceOptions = {}): Promise<GSDWorkspaceIndex> {
   139	  const milestoneIds = findMilestoneIds(basePath);
   140	  const milestones: WorkspaceMilestoneTarget[] = [];
   141	
   142	  for (const milestoneId of milestoneIds) {
   143	    const roadmapPath = resolveMilestoneFile(basePath, milestoneId, "ROADMAP") ?? undefined;
   144	    let title = milestoneId;
   145	    const slices: WorkspaceSliceTarget[] = [];
   146	
   147	    if (roadmapPath || isDbAvailable()) {
   148	      // Normalize slices from DB, fall back to file-based parsing when DB has no data
   149	      type NormSlice = { id: string; done: boolean; title: string; risk: string; depends: string[]; demo: string };
   150	      let normSlices: NormSlice[] | null = null;
   151	      if (isDbAvailable()) {
   152	        const dbSlices = getMilestoneSlices(milestoneId);
   153	        if (dbSlices.length > 0) {
   154	          normSlices = dbSlices.map(s => ({ id: s.id, done: s.status === "complete", title: s.title, risk: s.risk || "medium", depends: s.depends, demo: s.demo }));
   155	        }
   156	        // Get title from roadmap header
   157	        if (roadmapPath) {
   158	          const roadmapContent = await loadFile(roadmapPath);
   159	          if (roadmapContent) title = titleFromRoadmapHeader(roadmapContent, milestoneId);
   160	        }
   161	      }
   162	      if (!normSlices && roadmapPath) {
   163	        // File-based fallback: parse roadmap for slice entries
   164	        const roadmapContent = await loadFile(roadmapPath);
   165	        if (roadmapContent) {
   166	          title = titleFromRoadmapHeader(roadmapContent, milestoneId);
   167	          const parsed = parseRoadmap(roadmapContent);
   168	          normSlices = parsed.slices.map(s => ({ id: s.id, done: s.done, title: s.title, risk: s.risk || "medium", depends: s.depends, demo: s.demo || "" }));
   169	        }
   170	      }
   171	      if (!normSlices) normSlices = [];
   172	
   173	      if (normSlices.length > 0) {
   174	        const sliceResults = await Promise.all(
   175	          normSlices.map(async (slice) => {
   176	            return indexSlice(basePath, milestoneId, slice.id, slice.title, slice.done, { risk: slice.risk as RiskLevel, depends: slice.depends, demo: slice.demo });
   177	          }),
   178	        );
   179	
   180	        slices.push(...sliceResults);
   181	      }
   182	    }
   183	
   184	    milestones.push({ id: milestoneId, title, roadmapPath, slices });
   185	  }
   186	
   187	  const state = await deriveState(basePath);
   188	  const active = {
   189	    milestoneId: state.activeMilestone?.id,
   190	    sliceId: state.activeSlice?.id,
   191	    taskId: state.activeTask?.id,
   192	    phase: state.phase,
   193	  };
   194	
   195	  const scopes: WorkspaceScopeTarget[] = [{ scope: "project", label: "project", kind: "project" }];
   196	  for (const milestone of milestones) {
   197	    scopes.push({ scope: milestone.id, label: `${milestone.id}: ${milestone.title}`, kind: "milestone" });
   198	    for (const slice of milestone.slices) {
   199	      scopes.push({ scope: `${milestone.id}/${slice.id}`, label: `${milestone.id}/${slice.id}: ${slice.title}`, kind: "slice" });
   200	      for (const task of slice.tasks) {
   201	        scopes.push({
   202	          scope: `${milestone.id}/${slice.id}/${task.id}`,
   203	          label: `${milestone.id}/${slice.id}/${task.id}: ${task.title}`,
   204	          kind: "task",
   205	        });
   206	      }
   207	    }
   208	  }
   209	
   210	  return { milestones, active, scopes, validationIssues: [] };
   211	}
   212	
   213	export async function listDoctorScopeSuggestions(basePath: string): Promise<Array<{ value: string; label: string }>> {
   214	  const index = await indexWorkspace(basePath);
   215	  const activeSliceScope = index.active.milestoneId && index.active.sliceId
   216	    ? `${index.active.milestoneId}/${index.active.sliceId}`
   217	    : null;
   218	
   219	  const ordered = [...index.scopes].filter(scope => scope.kind !== "project");
   220	  ordered.sort((a, b) => {
   221	    if (activeSliceScope && a.scope === activeSliceScope) return -1;
   222	    if (activeSliceScope && b.scope === activeSliceScope) return 1;
   223	    return a.scope.localeCompare(b.scope);
   224	  });
   225	
   226	  return ordered.map(scope => ({ value: scope.scope, label: scope.label }));
   227	}
   228	
   229	export async function getSuggestedNextCommands(basePath: string): Promise<string[]> {
   230	  const index = await indexWorkspace(basePath);
   231	  const scope = index.active.milestoneId && index.active.sliceId
   232	    ? `${index.active.milestoneId}/${index.active.sliceId}`
   233	    : index.active.milestoneId;
   234	
   235	  const commands = new Set<string>();
   236	  if (index.active.phase === "planning") commands.add("/gsd");
   237	  if (index.active.phase === "executing" || index.active.phase === "summarizing") commands.add("/gsd auto");
   238	  if (scope) commands.add(`/gsd doctor ${scope}`);
   239	  if (scope) commands.add(`/gsd doctor fix ${scope}`);
   240	  commands.add("/gsd status");
   241	  return [...commands];
   242	}

    62	/**
    63	 * A "ghost" milestone directory contains only META.json (and no substantive
    64	 * files like CONTEXT, CONTEXT-DRAFT, ROADMAP, or SUMMARY).  These appear when
    65	 * a milestone is created but never initialised.  Treating them as active causes
    66	 * auto-mode to stall or falsely declare completion.
    67	 */
    68	export function isGhostMilestone(basePath: string, mid: string): boolean {
    69	  const context   = resolveMilestoneFile(basePath, mid, "CONTEXT");
    70	  const draft     = resolveMilestoneFile(basePath, mid, "CONTEXT-DRAFT");
    71	  const roadmap   = resolveMilestoneFile(basePath, mid, "ROADMAP");
    72	  const summary   = resolveMilestoneFile(basePath, mid, "SUMMARY");
    73	  return !context && !draft && !roadmap && !summary;
    74	}
    75	
    76	// ─── Query Functions ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    77	
    78	/**
    79	 * Check if all tasks in a slice plan are done.
    80	 */
    81	export function isSliceComplete(plan: SlicePlan): boolean {
    82	  return plan.tasks.length > 0 && plan.tasks.every(t => t.done);
    83	}
    84	
    85	/**
    86	 * Check if all slices in a roadmap are done.
    87	 */
    88	export function isMilestoneComplete(roadmap: Roadmap): boolean {
    89	  return roadmap.slices.length > 0 && roadmap.slices.every(s => s.done);
    90	}

    92	/**
    93	 * Check whether a VALIDATION file's verdict is terminal.
    94	 * Any successfully extracted verdict (pass, needs-attention, needs-remediation,
    95	 * fail, etc.) means validation completed. Only return false when no verdict
    96	 * could be parsed — i.e. extractVerdict() returns undefined (#2769).
    97	 */
    98	export function isValidationTerminal(validationContent: string): boolean {
    99	  return extractVerdict(validationContent) != null;
   100	}

   102	// ─── State Derivation ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────

   104	// ── deriveState memoization ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
   105	// Cache the most recent deriveState() result keyed by basePath. Within a single
   106	// dispatch cycle (~100ms window), repeated calls return the cached value instead
   107	// of re-reading the entire .gsd/ tree from disk.
   108	
   109	interface StateCache {
   110	  basePath: string;
   111	  result: GSDState;

   121	export function resetDeriveTelemetry() { _telemetry = { dbDeriveCount: 0, markdownDeriveCount: 0 }; }

   124	 * Invalidate the deriveState() cache. Call this whenever planning files on disk
   125	 * may have changed (unit completion, merges, file writes).
   126	 */
   127	export function invalidateStateCache(): void {
   128	  _stateCache = null;
   129	}

   131	/**
   132	 * Returns the ID of the first incomplete milestone, or null if all are complete.
   133	 */
   134	export async function getActiveMilestoneId(basePath: string): Promise<string | null> {
   135	  // Parallel worker isolation
   136	  const milestoneLock = process.env.GSD_MILESTONE_LOCK;
   137	  if (milestoneLock) {
   138	    const milestoneIds = findMilestoneIds(basePath);
   139	    if (!milestoneIds.includes(milestoneLock)) return null;
   140	    const lockedParked = resolveMilestoneFile(basePath, milestoneLock, "PARKED");
   141	    if (lockedParked) return null;
   142	    return milestoneLock;
   143	  }
   144	
   145	  // DB-first: query milestones table for the first non-complete, non-parked milestone
   146	  if (isDbAvailable()) {
   147	    const allMilestones = getAllMilestones();
   148	    if (allMilestones.length > 0) {
   149	      // Respect queue-order.json so /gsd queue reordering is honored (#2556).
   150	      // Without this, the DB path uses lexicographic sort while the dispatch
   151	      // guard uses queue order — causing a deadlock.
   152	      const customOrder = loadQueueOrder(basePath);
   153	      const sortedIds = sortByQueueOrder(allMilestones.map(m => m.id), customOrder);
   154	      const byId = new Map(allMilestones.map(m => [m.id, m]));
   155	      for (const id of sortedIds) {
   156	        const m = byId.get(id)!;
   157	        if (m.status === "complete" || m.status === "done" || m.status === "parked") continue;
   158	        return m.id;
   159	      }
   160	      return null;
   161	    }
   162	  }
   163	
   164	  // Filesystem fallback for unmigrated projects or empty DB
   165	  const milestoneIds = findMilestoneIds(basePath);
   166	  for (const mid of milestoneIds) {
   167	    const parkedFile = resolveMilestoneFile(basePath, mid, "PARKED");
   168	    if (parkedFile) continue;
   169	
   170	    const roadmapFile = resolveMilestoneFile(basePath, mid, "ROADMAP");
   171	    const content = roadmapFile ? await loadFile(roadmapFile) : null;
   172	    if (!content) {
   173	      const summaryFile = resolveMilestoneFile(basePath, mid, "SUMMARY");
   174	      if (summaryFile) continue;
   175	      if (isGhostMilestone(basePath, mid)) continue;
   176	      return mid;
   177	    }
   178	    const roadmap = parseRoadmap(content);
   179	    if (!isMilestoneComplete(roadmap)) {
   180	      const summaryFile = resolveMilestoneFile(basePath, mid, "SUMMARY");
   181	      if (!summaryFile) return mid;
   182	    }
   183	  }
   184	  return null;
   185	}

   187	/**
   188	 * Reconstruct GSD state from DB (primary) or filesystem (fallback).
   189	 * STATE.md is a rendered cache of this output.
   190	 *
   191	 * When DB is available, queries milestone/slice/task tables directly.
   192	 * Falls back to filesystem parsing for unmigrated projects or when DB
   193	 * has zero milestones (e.g. first run before migration).
   194	 */
   195	export async function deriveState(basePath: string): Promise<GSDState> {
   196	  // Return cached result if within the TTL window for the same basePath
   197	  if (
   198	    _stateCache &&
   199	    _stateCache.basePath === basePath &&
   200	    Date.now() - _stateCache.timestamp < CACHE_TTL_MS
   201	  ) {
   202	    return _stateCache.result;
   203	  }
   204	
   205	  const stopTimer = debugTime("derive-state-impl");
   206	  let result: GSDState;
   207	
   208	  // Dual-path: try DB-backed derivation first when hierarchy tables are populated
   209	  if (isDbAvailable()) {
   210	    let dbMilestones = getAllMilestones();
   211	
   212	    // Disk→DB reconciliation (#2631): when the milestones table is empty
   213	    // (e.g. failed initial migration per #2529), the reconciliation code
   214	    // inside deriveStateFromDb is unreachable. Populate from disk here so
   215	    // the DB path activates correctly.
   216	    if (dbMilestones.length === 0) {
   217	      const diskIds = findMilestoneIds(basePath);
   218	      let synced = false;
   219	      for (const diskId of diskIds) {
   220	        if (!isGhostMilestone(basePath, diskId)) {
   221	          insertMilestone({ id: diskId, status: 'active' });
   222	          synced = true;
   223	        }
   224	      }
   225	      if (synced) dbMilestones = getAllMilestones();
   226	    }
   227	
   228	    if (dbMilestones.length > 0) {
   229	      const stopDbTimer = debugTime("derive-state-db");
   230	      result = await deriveStateFromDb(basePath);
   231	      stopDbTimer({ phase: result.phase, milestone: result.activeMilestone?.id });
   232	      _telemetry.dbDeriveCount++;
   233	    } else {
   234	      // DB open but empty hierarchy tables — pre-migration project, use filesystem
   235	      result = await _deriveStateImpl(basePath);
   236	      _telemetry.markdownDeriveCount++;
   237	    }
   238	  } else {
   239	    result = await _deriveStateImpl(basePath);
   240	    _telemetry.markdownDeriveCount++;
   241	  }
   242	
   243	  stopTimer({ phase: result.phase, milestone: result.activeMilestone?.id });
   244	  debugCount("deriveStateCalls");
   245	  _stateCache = { basePath, result, timestamp: Date.now() };
   246	  return result;
   247	}
   248	
   249	/**
   250	 * Extract milestone title from CONTEXT.md or CONTEXT-DRAFT.md heading.
   251	 * Falls back to the provided fallback (usually the milestone ID).
   252	 */
   253	/**
   254	 * Strip the "M001: " prefix from a milestone title to get the human-readable name.
   255	 * Used by both DB and filesystem paths for consistency.
   256	 */
   257	function stripMilestonePrefix(title: string): string {
   258	  return title.replace(/^M\d+(?:-[a-z0-9]{6})?[^:]*:\s*/, '') || title;
   259	}
   260	
   261	function extractContextTitle(content: string | null, fallback: string): string {
   262	  if (!content) return fallback;
   263	  const h1 = content.split('\n').find(line => line.startsWith('# '));
   264	  if (!h1) return fallback;
   265	  // Extract title from "# M005: Platform Foundation & Separation" format
   266	  return stripMilestonePrefix(h1.slice(2).trim()) || fallback;
   267	}
   268	
   269	// ─── DB-backed State Derivation ────────────────────────────────────────────
   270	
   271	/**
   272	 * Derive GSD state from the milestones/slices/tasks DB tables.
   273	 * Flag files (PARKED, VALIDATION, CONTINUE, REPLAN, REPLAN-TRIGGER, CONTEXT-DRAFT)
   274	 * are still checked on the filesystem since they aren't in DB tables.
   275	 * Requirements also stay file-based via parseRequirementCounts().
   276	 *
   277	 * Must produce field-identical GSDState to _deriveStateImpl() for the same project.
   278	 */
   279	export async function deriveStateFromDb(basePath: string): Promise<GSDState> {
   280	  const requirements = parseRequirementCounts(await loadFile(resolveGsdRootFile(basePath, "REQUIREMENTS")));
   281	
   282	  let allMilestones = getAllMilestones();
   283	
   284	  // Incremental disk→DB sync: milestone directories created outside the DB
   285	  // write path (via /gsd queue, manual mkdir, or complete-milestone writing the
   286	  // next CONTEXT.md) are never inserted by the initial migration guard in
   287	  // auto-start.ts because that guard only runs when gsd.db doesn't exist yet.
   288	  // Reconcile here so deriveStateFromDb never silently misses queued milestones.
   289	  // insertMilestone uses INSERT OR IGNORE, so this is safe to call every time.
   290	  const dbIdSet = new Set(allMilestones.map(m => m.id));
   291	  const diskIds = findMilestoneIds(basePath);
   292	  let synced = false;
   293	  for (const diskId of diskIds) {
   294	    if (!dbIdSet.has(diskId) && !isGhostMilestone(basePath, diskId)) {
   295	      insertMilestone({ id: diskId, status: 'active' });
   296	      synced = true;
   297	    }
   298	  }
   299	  if (synced) allMilestones = getAllMilestones();
   300	
   301	  // Reconcile: discover milestones that exist on disk but are missing from
   302	  // the DB. This happens when milestones were created before the DB migration
   303	  // or were manually added to the filesystem. Without this, disk-only
   304	  // milestones are invisible after migration (#2416).
   305	  const dbMilestoneIds = new Set(allMilestones.map(m => m.id));
   306	  const diskMilestoneIds = findMilestoneIds(basePath);
   307	  for (const diskId of diskMilestoneIds) {
   308	    if (!dbMilestoneIds.has(diskId)) {
   309	      // Synthesize a minimal MilestoneRow for the disk-only milestone.
   310	      // Title and status will be resolved from disk files in the loop below.
   311	      allMilestones.push({
   312	        id: diskId,
   313	        title: diskId,
   314	        status: 'active',
   315	        depends_on: [] as string[],
   316	        created_at: new Date().toISOString(),
   317	      } as MilestoneRow);
   318	    }
   319	  }
   320	  // Re-sort so milestones follow queue order (same as dispatch guard) (#2556)
   321	  const customOrder = loadQueueOrder(basePath);
   322	  const sortedIds = sortByQueueOrder(allMilestones.map(m => m.id), customOrder);
   323	  const byId = new Map(allMilestones.map(m => [m.id, m]));
   324	  allMilestones.length = 0;
   325	  for (const id of sortedIds) allMilestones.push(byId.get(id)!);
   326	
   327	  // Parallel worker isolation: when locked, filter to just the locked milestone
   328	  const milestoneLock = process.env.GSD_MILESTONE_LOCK;
   329	  const milestones = milestoneLock
   330	    ? allMilestones.filter(m => m.id === milestoneLock)
   331	    : allMilestones;
   332	
   333	  if (milestones.length === 0) {
   334	    return {
   335	      activeMilestone: null,
   336	      activeSlice: null,
   337	      activeTask: null,
   338	      phase: 'pre-planning',
   339	      recentDecisions: [],
   340	      blockers: [],
   341	      nextAction: 'No milestones found. Run /gsd to create one.',
   342	      registry: [],
   343	      requirements,
   344	      progress: { milestones: { done: 0, total: 0 } },
   345	    };
   346	  }
   347	
   348	  // Phase 1: Build completeness set (which milestones count as "done" for dep resolution)
   349	  const completeMilestoneIds = new Set<string>();
   350	  const parkedMilestoneIds = new Set<string>();
   351	
   352	  for (const m of milestones) {
   353	    // Check disk for PARKED flag (not stored in DB status reliably — disk is truth for flag files)
   354	    const parkedFile = resolveMilestoneFile(basePath, m.id, "PARKED");
   355	    if (parkedFile || m.status === 'parked') {
   356	      parkedMilestoneIds.add(m.id);
   357	      continue;
   358	    }
   359	
   360	    if (isClosedStatus(m.status)) {
   361	      completeMilestoneIds.add(m.id);
   362	      continue;
   363	    }
   364	
   365	    // Check if milestone has a summary on disk (terminal artifact per #864)
   366	    const summaryFile = resolveMilestoneFile(basePath, m.id, "SUMMARY");
   367	    if (summaryFile) {
   368	      completeMilestoneIds.add(m.id);
   369	      continue;
   370	    }
   371	
   372	    // Check roadmap: all slices done means milestone is complete
   373	    const slices = getMilestoneSlices(m.id);
   374	    if (slices.length > 0 && slices.every(s => isClosedStatus(s.status))) {
   375	      // All slices done but no summary — still counts as complete for dep resolution
   376	      // if a summary file exists
   377	      // Note: without summary file, the milestone is in validating/completing state, not complete
   378	    }
   379	  }
   380	
   381	  // Phase 2: Build registry and find active milestone
   382	  const registry: MilestoneRegistryEntry[] = [];
   383	  let activeMilestone: ActiveRef | null = null;
   384	  let activeMilestoneSlices: SliceRow[] = [];
   385	  let activeMilestoneFound = false;
   386	  let activeMilestoneHasDraft = false;
   387	
   388	  for (const m of milestones) {
   389	    if (parkedMilestoneIds.has(m.id)) {
   390	      registry.push({ id: m.id, title: stripMilestonePrefix(m.title) || m.id, status: 'parked' });
   391	      continue;
   392	    }
   393	
   394	    // Ghost milestone check: no slices in DB AND no substantive files on disk
   395	    const slices = getMilestoneSlices(m.id);
   396	    if (slices.length === 0 && !isClosedStatus(m.status)) {
   397	      // Check disk for ghost detection
   398	      if (isGhostMilestone(basePath, m.id)) continue;
   399	    }
   400	
   401	    const summaryFile = resolveMilestoneFile(basePath, m.id, "SUMMARY");
   402	
   403	    // Determine if this milestone is complete
   404	    if (completeMilestoneIds.has(m.id) || (summaryFile !== null)) {
   405	      // Get title from DB or summary
   406	      let title = stripMilestonePrefix(m.title) || m.id;
   407	      if (summaryFile && !m.title) {
   408	        const summaryContent = await loadFile(summaryFile);
   409	        if (summaryContent) {
   410	          title = parseSummary(summaryContent).title || m.id;
   411	        }
   412	      }
   413	      registry.push({ id: m.id, title, status: 'complete' });
   414	      completeMilestoneIds.add(m.id); // ensure it's in the set
   415	      continue;
   416	    }
   417	
   418	    // Not complete — determine if it should be active
   419	    const allSlicesDone = slices.length > 0 && slices.every(s => isClosedStatus(s.status));
   420	
   421	    // Get title — prefer DB, fall back to context file extraction
   422	    let title = stripMilestonePrefix(m.title) || m.id;
   423	    if (title === m.id) {
   424	      const contextFile = resolveMilestoneFile(basePath, m.id, "CONTEXT");
   425	      const draftFile = resolveMilestoneFile(basePath, m.id, "CONTEXT-DRAFT");
   426	      const contextContent = contextFile ? await loadFile(contextFile) : null;
   427	      const draftContent = draftFile && !contextContent ? await loadFile(draftFile) : null;
   428	      title = extractContextTitle(contextContent || draftContent, m.id);
   429	    }
   430

   390	  cycleCounts: Record<string, number>;
   391	  /** Timestamp of last state save. */
   392	  savedAt: string;
   393	}
   394	
   395	export interface HookStatusEntry {
   396	  /** Hook name. */
   397	  name: string;
   398	  /** Hook type: "post" or "pre". */
   399	  type: "post" | "pre";
   400	  /** Whether hook is enabled. */
   401	  enabled: boolean;
   402	  /** What unit types it targets. */
   403	  targets: string[];
   404	  /** Current cycle counts for active triggers. */
   405	  activeCycles: Record<string, number>;

   410	export type DecisionMadeBy = "human" | "agent" | "collaborative";
   411	
   412	export interface Decision {
   413	  seq: number; // auto-increment primary key
   414	  id: string; // e.g. "D001"
   415	  when_context: string; // when/context of the decision
   416	  scope: string; // scope (milestone, slice, global, etc.)

   419	  rationale: string; // why this choice

   422	  superseded_by: string | null; // ID of superseding decision, or null
   423	}
   424	
   425	export interface Requirement {
   426	  id: string; // e.g. "R001"
   427	  class: string; // requirement class (functional, non-functional, etc.)
   428	  status: string; // active, validated, deferred, etc.

   430	  why: string; // rationale
   431	  source: string; // origin (milestone, user, etc.)
   432	  primary_owner: string; // owning slice/milestone

   434	  validation: string; // how to validate
   435	  notes: string; // additional notes
   436	  full_content: string; // full requirement text
   437	  superseded_by: string | null; // ID of superseding requirement, or null
   438	}

   574	  const allSlicesDone = activeMilestoneSlices.length > 0 && activeMilestoneSlices.every(s => isClosedStatus(s.status));

   576	    const validationFile = resolveMilestoneFile(basePath, activeMilestone.id, "VALIDATION");
   577	    const validationContent = validationFile ? await loadFile(validationFile) : null;
   578	    const validationTerminal = validationContent ? isValidationTerminal(validationContent) : false;
   579	    const sliceProgress = {
   580	      done: activeMilestoneSlices.length,
   581	      total: activeMilestoneSlices.length,
   582	    };
   583	
   584	    if (!validationTerminal) {

   586	        activeMilestone, activeSlice: null, activeTask: null,
   587	        phase: 'validating-milestone',

   590	        registry, requirements,
   591	        progress: { milestones: milestoneProgress, slices: sliceProgress },
   592	      };
   593	    }
   594	
   595	    return {
   596	      activeMilestone, activeSlice: null, activeTask: null,
   597	      phase: 'completing-milestone',
   598	      recentDecisions: [], blockers: [],
   599	      nextAction: `All slices complete in ${activeMilestone.id}. Write milestone summary.`,
   600	      registry, requirements,
   601	      progress: { milestones: milestoneProgress, slices: sliceProgress },
   602	    };
   603	  }

   606	  const sliceProgress = {
   607	    done: activeMilestoneSlices.filter(s => isClosedStatus(s.status)).length,
   608	    total: activeMilestoneSlices.length,
   609	  };
   610	
   611	  const doneSliceIds = new Set(
   612	    activeMilestoneSlices.filter(s => isClosedStatus(s.status)).map(s => s.id)
   613	  );
   614	
   615	  let activeSlice: ActiveRef | null = null;
   616	  let activeSliceRow: SliceRow | null = null;
   617

   619	    if (isClosedStatus(s.status)) continue;
   620	    if (s.depends.every(dep => doneSliceIds.has(dep))) {
   621	      activeSlice = { id: s.id, title: s.title };
   622	      activeSliceRow = s;
   623	      break;
   624	    }
   625	  }
   626	
   627	  if (!activeSlice) {
   628	    return {
   629	      activeMilestone, activeSlice: null, activeTask: null,
   630	      phase: 'blocked',
   631	      recentDecisions: [], blockers: ['No slice eligible — check dependency ordering'],

   633	      registry, requirements,

   636	  }

   639	  const planFile = resolveSliceFile(basePath, activeMilestone.id, activeSlice.id, "PLAN");
   640	  if (!planFile) {

   642	      activeMilestone, activeSlice, activeTask: null,
   643	      phase: 'planning',

     1	/**
     2	 * Status predicates for GSD state-machine guards.
     3	 *
     4	 * The DB stores status as free-form strings. Two values indicate
     5	 * "closed": "complete" (canonical) and "done" (legacy / alias).
     6	 * Every inline `status === "complete" || status === "done"` should
     7	 * use isClosedStatus() instead.
     8	 */

    10	/** Returns true when a milestone, slice, or task status indicates closure. */
    11	export function isClosedStatus(status: string): boolean {
    12	  return status === "complete" || status === "done";

     1	/**
     2	 * Centralized verdict extraction, normalization, and schema validation.
     3	 *
     4	 * All verdict-related logic lives here so that normalization rules
     5	 * (e.g. `passed` → `pass`) are applied consistently across the codebase.
     6	 */
     7	
     8	import { extractUatType } from "./files.js";
     9	import type { UatType } from "./files.js";
    10	
    11	// ── Verdict extraction ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
    12	
    13	/**
    14	 * Extract and normalize the `verdict` value from YAML frontmatter.
    15	 *
    16	 * Normalization:
    17	 * - lowercased
    18	 * - `passed` → `pass`
    19	 *
    20	 * Returns `undefined` when frontmatter is absent or has no `verdict` field.
    21	 */
    22	export function extractVerdict(content: string): string | undefined {
    23	  const fmMatch = content.match(/^---\n([\s\S]*?)\n---/);
    24	  if (!fmMatch) return undefined;
    25	  const verdictMatch = fmMatch[1].match(/verdict:\s*([\w-]+)/i);
    26	  if (!verdictMatch) return undefined;
    27	  let v = verdictMatch[1].toLowerCase();
    28	  if (v === "passed") v = "pass";
    29	  return v;
    30	}
    31	
    32	/**
    33	 * Returns `true` when the content's frontmatter contains a `verdict` field.
    34	 */
    35	export function hasVerdict(content: string): boolean {
    36	  return /verdict:\s*[\w-]+/i.test(content);
    37	}
    38	
    39	// ── UAT verdict schema ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
    40	
    41	/**
    42	 * Base verdicts that are always acceptable for UAT results.
    43	 */
    44	export const UAT_ACCEPTABLE_VERDICTS: readonly string[] = ["pass", "passed"];
    45	
    46	/**
    47	 * UAT types whose results may legitimately produce a `partial` verdict
    48	 * when all automatable checks pass but human-only checks remain.
    49	 */
    50	const PARTIAL_ELIGIBLE_UAT_TYPES: readonly UatType[] = [
    51	  "mixed",
    52	  "human-experience",
    53	  "live-runtime",
    54	];
    55	
    56	/**
    57	 * Check whether a verdict is acceptable for a given UAT type.
    58	 *
    59	 * `pass` / `passed` are always acceptable. `partial` is acceptable only for
    60	 * UAT types that include non-automatable human checks.
    61	 */
    62	export function isAcceptableUatVerdict(verdict: string, uatType: UatType | undefined): boolean {
    63	  if (UAT_ACCEPTABLE_VERDICTS.includes(verdict)) return true;
    64	  if (verdict === "partial" && uatType && (PARTIAL_ELIGIBLE_UAT_TYPES as readonly string[]).includes(uatType)) {
    65	    return true;
    66	  }
    67	  return false;
    68	}
    69	
    70	// ── Milestone validation verdict schema ─────────────────────────────────
    71	
    72	/**
    73	 * Valid verdicts for the `validate-milestone` tool.
    74	 */
    75	export const VALIDATION_VERDICTS = ["pass", "needs-attention", "needs-remediation"] as const;
    76	export type ValidationVerdict = (typeof VALIDATION_VERDICTS)[number];
    77	
    78	/**
    79	 * Check whether a string is a valid milestone validation verdict.
    80	 */
    81	export function isValidMilestoneVerdict(verdict: string): verdict is ValidationVerdict {
    82	  return (VALIDATION_VERDICTS as readonly string[]).includes(verdict);
    83	}
    84	
    85	// ── UAT type helper ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    86	
    87	/**
    88	 * Extract the UAT type from content, defaulting to `"artifact-driven"`.
    89	 *
    90	 * The `"artifact-driven"` fallback is the original default used throughout
    91	 * the codebase when a UAT file lacks an explicit `## UAT Type` section.
    92	 */
    93	export function getUatType(content: string): UatType {
    94	  return extractUatType(content) ?? "artifact-driven";
    95	}
    96

   152	/** Format a USD cost value — uses more decimals for small amounts. */
   153	export function formatCost(cost: number): string {
   154	  const n = Number(cost) || 0
   155	  if (n < 0.01) return `$${n.toFixed(4)}`
   156	  if (n < 1) return `$${n.toFixed(3)}`
   157	  return `$${n.toFixed(2)}`
   158	}
   159	
   160	/** Format a token count with K/M suffixes for readability. */
   161	export function formatTokenCount(count: number): string {
   162	  if (count < 1000) return `${count}`
   163	  if (count < 1_000_000) return `${(count / 1000).toFixed(1)}K`
   164	  return `${(count / 1_000_000).toFixed(2)}M`
   165	}
   166	
   167	/** Format a duration in milliseconds as human-readable Xs / Xm Xs / Xh Xm. */
   168	export function formatDuration(ms: number): string {
   169	  const totalSeconds = Math.round(ms / 1000)
   170	  if (totalSeconds < 60) return `${totalSeconds}s`
   171	  const minutes = Math.floor(totalSeconds / 60)
   172	  const seconds = totalSeconds % 60
   173	  if (minutes < 60) {
   174	    return seconds > 0 ? `${minutes}m ${seconds}s` : `${minutes}m`
   175	  }
   176	  const hours = Math.floor(minutes / 60)
   177	  const remainingMinutes = minutes % 60
   178	  return remainingMinutes > 0 ? `${hours}h ${remainingMinutes}m` : `${hours}h`
   179	}

   231	// ─── Critical Path ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   232	
   233	export function computeCriticalPath(milestones: VisualizerMilestone[]): CriticalPathInfo {
   234	  const empty: CriticalPathInfo = {
   235	    milestonePath: [],
   236	    slicePath: [],
   237	    milestoneSlack: new Map(),
   238	    sliceSlack: new Map(),
   239	  };
   240	
   241	  if (milestones.length === 0) return empty;
   242	
   243	  // Milestone-level critical path (weight = number of incomplete slices)
   244	  const msMap = new Map(milestones.map(m => [m.id, m]));
   245	  const msIds = milestones.map(m => m.id);
   246	  const msAdj = new Map<string, string[]>();
   247	  const msWeight = new Map<string, number>();
   248	
   249	  for (const ms of milestones) {
   250	    msAdj.set(ms.id, []);
   251	    const incomplete = ms.slices.filter(s => !s.done).length;
   252	    msWeight.set(ms.id, ms.status === 'complete' ? 0 : Math.max(1, incomplete));
   253	  }
   254	
   255	  for (const ms of milestones) {
   256	    for (const dep of ms.dependsOn) {
   257	      if (msMap.has(dep)) {
   258	        const adj = msAdj.get(dep);
   259	        if (adj) adj.push(ms.id);
   260	      }
   261	    }
   262	  }
   263	
   264	  // Topological sort (Kahn's algorithm)
   265	  const inDegree = new Map<string, number>();
   266	  for (const id of msIds) inDegree.set(id, 0);
   267	  for (const ms of milestones) {
   268	    for (const dep of ms.dependsOn) {
   269	      if (msMap.has(dep)) inDegree.set(ms.id, (inDegree.get(ms.id) ?? 0) + 1);
   270	    }
   271	  }
   272	
   273	  const queue: string[] = [];
   274	  for (const [id, deg] of inDegree) {
   275	    if (deg === 0) queue.push(id);
   276	  }
   277	
   278	  const topoOrder: string[] = [];
   279	  while (queue.length > 0) {
   280	    const node = queue.shift()!;
   281	    topoOrder.push(node);
   282	    for (const next of (msAdj.get(node) ?? [])) {
   283	      const d = (inDegree.get(next) ?? 1) - 1;
   284	      inDegree.set(next, d);
   285	      if (d === 0) queue.push(next);
   286	    }
   287	  }
   288	
   289	  // Longest path from each root
   290	  const dist = new Map<string, number>();
   291	  const prev = new Map<string, string | null>();
   292	  for (const id of msIds) {
   293	    dist.set(id, 0);
   294	    prev.set(id, null);
   295	  }
   296	
   297	  for (const node of topoOrder) {
   298	    const w = msWeight.get(node) ?? 1;
   299	    const nodeDist = dist.get(node)! + w;
   300	    for (const next of (msAdj.get(node) ?? [])) {
   301	      if (nodeDist > dist.get(next)!) {
   302	        dist.set(next, nodeDist);
   303	        prev.set(next, node);
   304	      }
   305	    }
   306	  }
   307	
   308	  // Find the end of the critical path (node with max dist + own weight)
   309	  let maxDist = 0;
   310	  let endNode = msIds[0];
   311	  for (const id of msIds) {
   312	    const totalDist = dist.get(id)! + (msWeight.get(id) ?? 1);
   313	    if (totalDist > maxDist) {
   314	      maxDist = totalDist;
   315	      endNode = id;
   316	    }
   317	  }
   318	
   319	  // Trace back
   320	  const milestonePath: string[] = [];
   321	  let cur: string | null = endNode;
   322	  while (cur !== null) {
   323	    milestonePath.unshift(cur);
   324	    cur = prev.get(cur) ?? null;
   325	  }
   326	
   327	  // Compute milestone slack
   328	  const milestoneSlack = new Map<string, number>();
   329	  const criticalSet = new Set(milestonePath);
   330	  for (const id of msIds) {
   331	    if (criticalSet.has(id)) {
   332	      milestoneSlack.set(id, 0);
   333	    } else {
   334	      const nodeTotal = dist.get(id)! + (msWeight.get(id) ?? 1);
   335	      milestoneSlack.set(id, Math.max(0, maxDist - nodeTotal));
   336	    }
   337	  }
   338	
   339	  // Slice-level critical path within active milestone
   340	  const activeMs = milestones.find(m => m.status === 'active');
   341	  let slicePath: string[] = [];
   342	  const sliceSlack = new Map<string, number>();
   343	
   344	  if (activeMs && activeMs.slices.length > 0) {
   345	    const slMap = new Map(activeMs.slices.map(s => [s.id, s]));
   346	    const slAdj = new Map<string, string[]>();
   347	    for (const s of activeMs.slices) slAdj.set(s.id, []);
   348	    for (const s of activeMs.slices) {
   349	      for (const dep of s.depends) {
   350	        if (slMap.has(dep)) {
   351	          const adj = slAdj.get(dep);
   352	          if (adj) adj.push(s.id);
   353	        }
   354	      }
   355	    }
   356	
   357	    // Topo sort slices
   358	    const slIn = new Map<string, number>();
   359	    for (const s of activeMs.slices) slIn.set(s.id, 0);
   360	    for (const s of activeMs.slices) {
   361	      for (const dep of s.depends) {
   362	        if (slMap.has(dep)) slIn.set(s.id, (slIn.get(s.id) ?? 0) + 1);
   363	      }
   364	    }
   365	
   366	    const slQueue: string[] = [];
   367	    for (const [id, d] of slIn) {
   368	      if (d === 0) slQueue.push(id);
   369	    }
   370	
   371	    const slTopo: string[] = [];
   372	    while (slQueue.length > 0) {
   373	      const n = slQueue.shift()!;
   374	      slTopo.push(n);
   375	      for (const next of (slAdj.get(n) ?? [])) {
   376	        const d = (slIn.get(next) ?? 1) - 1;
   377	        slIn.set(next, d);
   378	        if (d === 0) slQueue.push(next);
   379	      }
   380	    }
   381	
   382	    const slDist = new Map<string, number>();
   383	    const slPrev = new Map<string, string | null>();
   384	    for (const s of activeMs.slices) {
   385	      const w = s.done ? 0 : 1;
   386	      slDist.set(s.id, 0);
   387	      slPrev.set(s.id, null);
   388	    }
   389	
   390	    for (const n of slTopo) {
   391	      const w = (slMap.get(n)?.done ? 0 : 1);
   392	      const nd = slDist.get(n)! + w;
   393	      for (const next of (slAdj.get(n) ?? [])) {
   394	        if (nd > slDist.get(next)!) {
   395	          slDist.set(next, nd);
   396	          slPrev.set(next, n);
   397	        }
   398	      }
   399	    }
   400	
   401	    let slMax = 0;
   402	    let slEnd = activeMs.slices[0].id;
   403	    for (const s of activeMs.slices) {
   404	      const totalDist = slDist.get(s.id)! + (s.done ? 0 : 1);
   405	      if (totalDist > slMax) {
   406	        slMax = totalDist;
   407	        slEnd = s.id;
   408	      }
   409	    }
   410	
   411	    let slCur: string | null = slEnd;
   412	    while (slCur !== null) {
   413	      slicePath.unshift(slCur);
   414	      slCur = slPrev.get(slCur) ?? null;
   415	    }
   416	
   417	    const slCritSet = new Set(slicePath);
   418	    for (const s of activeMs.slices) {
   419	      if (slCritSet.has(s.id)) {
   420	        sliceSlack.set(s.id, 0);
   421	      } else {
   422	        const nodeTotal = slDist.get(s.id)! + (s.done ? 0 : 1);
   423	        sliceSlack.set(s.id, Math.max(0, slMax - nodeTotal));
   424	      }
   425	    }
   426	  }
   427	
   428	  return { milestonePath, slicePath, milestoneSlack, sliceSlack };
   429	}
   430	
   431	// ─── Agent Activity ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   432	
   433	function loadAgentActivity(units: UnitMetrics[], milestones: VisualizerMilestone[]): AgentActivityInfo | null {
   434	  if (units.length === 0) return null;
   435	
   436	  // Find currently running unit (finishedAt === 0)
   437	  const running = units.find(u => u.finishedAt === 0);
   438	  const now = Date.now();
   439	
   440	  const completedUnits = units.filter(u => u.finishedAt > 0).length;
   441	  const totalSlices = milestones.reduce((sum, m) => sum + m.slices.length, 0);
   442	
   443	  // Completion rate from finished units
   444	  const finished = units.filter(u => u.finishedAt > 0);
   445	  let completionRate = 0;
   446	  if (finished.length >= 2) {
   447	    const earliest = Math.min(...finished.map(u => u.startedAt));
   448	    const latest = Math.max(...finished.map(u => u.finishedAt));
   449	    const totalHours = (latest - earliest) / 3_600_000;
   450	    completionRate = totalHours > 0 ? finished.length / totalHours : 0;
   451	  }
   452	
   453	  const sessionCost = units.reduce((sum, u) => sum + u.cost, 0);
   454	  const sessionTokens = units.reduce((sum, u) => sum + u.tokens.total, 0);
   455	
   456	  return {
   457	    currentUnit: running
   458	      ? { type: running.type, id: running.id, startedAt: running.startedAt }
   459	      : null,
   460	    elapsed: running ? now - running.startedAt : 0,
   461	    completedUnits,
   462	    totalSlices,
   463	    completionRate,
   464	    active: !!running,
   465	    sessionCost,
   466	    sessionTokens,
   467	  };
   468	}
   469	
   470	// ─── Changelog & Verifications ────────────────────────────────────────────────
   471	
   472	const changelogCache = new Map<string, { mtime: number; entry: ChangelogEntry; verification: SliceVerification }>();
   473	
   474	interface ChangelogAndVerifications {
   475	  changelog: ChangelogInfo;
   476	  verifications: SliceVerification[];
   477	}
   478	
   479	async function loadChangelogAndVerifications(basePath: string, milestones: VisualizerMilestone[]): Promise<ChangelogAndVerifications> {
   480	  const entries: ChangelogEntry[] = [];
   481	  const verifications: SliceVerification[] = [];
   482	
   483	  for (const ms of milestones) {
   484	    for (const sl of ms.slices) {
   485	      if (!sl.done) continue;
   486	
   487	      const summaryFile = resolveSliceFile(basePath, ms.id, sl.id, 'SUMMARY');
   488	      if (!summaryFile) continue;
   489	
   490	      const cacheKey = `${ms.id}/${sl.id}`;
   491	      const cached = changelogCache.get(cacheKey);
   492	
   493	      let mtime = 0;
   494	      try {
   495	        mtime = statSync(summaryFile).mtimeMs;
   496	      } catch {
   497	        continue;
   498	      }
   499	
   500	      if (cached && cached.mtime === mtime) {
   501	        entries.push(cached.entry);
   502	        verifications.push(cached.verification);
   503	        continue;
   504	      }
   505	
   506	      const content = await loadFile(summaryFile);
   507	      if (!content) continue;
   508	
   509	      const summary = parseSummary(content);
   510	      const entry: ChangelogEntry = {
   511	        milestoneId: ms.id,
   512	        sliceId: sl.id,
   513	        title: sl.title,
   514	        oneLiner: summary.oneLiner,
   515	        filesModified: summary.filesModified.map(f => ({
   516	          path: f.path,
   517	          description: f.description,
   518	        })),
   519	        completedAt: String(summary.frontmatter.completed_at ?? ''),
   520	      };
   521	
   522	      const verification: SliceVerification = {
   523	        milestoneId: ms.id,
   524	        sliceId: sl.id,
   525	        verificationResult: summary.frontmatter.verification_result || '',
   526	        blockerDiscovered: summary.frontmatter.blocker_discovered,
   527	        keyDecisions: summary.frontmatter.key_decisions || [],
   528	        patternsEstablished: summary.frontmatter.patterns_established || [],
   529	        provides: summary.frontmatter.provides || [],
   530	        requires: (summary.frontmatter.requires || []).map(r => ({
   531	          slice: r.slice,
   532	          provides: r.provides,
   533	        })),
   534	      };
   535	
   536	      changelogCache.set(cacheKey, { mtime, entry, verification });
   537	      entries.push(entry);
   538	      verifications.push(verification);
   539	    }
   540	  }
   541	
   542	  entries.sort((a, b) => String(b.completedAt || '').localeCompare(String(a.completedAt || '')));
   543	
   544	  return { changelog: { entries }, verifications };
   545	}

   785	export async function loadVisualizerData(basePath: string): Promise<VisualizerData> {
   786	  const state = await deriveState(basePath);
   787	  const milestoneIds = findMilestoneIds(basePath);
   788	
   789	  const milestones: VisualizerMilestone[] = [];
   790	
   791	  for (const mid of milestoneIds) {
   792	    const entry = state.registry.find(r => r.id === mid);
   793	    const status = entry?.status ?? 'pending';
   794	    const dependsOn = entry?.dependsOn ?? [];
   795	
   796	    const slices: VisualizerSlice[] = [];
   797	
   798	    const roadmapFile = resolveMilestoneFile(basePath, mid, 'ROADMAP');
   799	    const roadmapContent = roadmapFile ? readFileCached(roadmapFile) : null;
   800	
   801	    if (roadmapContent || isDbAvailable()) {
   802	      // Normalize slices from DB, fall back to file-based parsing when DB has no data
   803	      type NormSlice = { id: string; done: boolean; title: string; risk: string; depends: string[]; demo: string };
   804	      let normSlices: NormSlice[] | null = null;
   805	      if (isDbAvailable()) {
   806	        const dbSlices = getMilestoneSlices(mid);
   807	        if (dbSlices.length > 0) {
   808	          normSlices = dbSlices.map(s => ({ id: s.id, done: s.status === 'complete', title: s.title, risk: s.risk || 'medium', depends: s.depends, demo: s.demo }));
   809	        }
   810	      }
   811	      if (!normSlices && roadmapContent) {
   812	        // File-based fallback: parse roadmap for slice entries
   813	        const parsed = parseRoadmap(roadmapContent);
   814	        normSlices = parsed.slices.map(s => ({ id: s.id, done: s.done, title: s.title, risk: s.risk || 'medium', depends: s.depends, demo: '' }));
   815	      }
   816	      if (!normSlices) normSlices = [];
   817	
   818	      for (const s of normSlices) {
   819	        const isActiveSlice =
   820	          state.activeMilestone?.id === mid &&
   821	          state.activeSlice?.id === s.id;
   822	
   823	        const tasks: VisualizerTask[] = [];
   824

   826	          // Normalize tasks from DB, fall back to file parsing when DB has no data
   827	          let usedDbTasks = false;
   828	          if (isDbAvailable()) {
   829	            const dbTasks = getSliceTasks(mid, s.id);
   830	            if (dbTasks.length > 0) {
   831	              usedDbTasks = true;
   832	              for (const t of dbTasks) {
   833	                tasks.push({
   834	                  id: t.id,
   835	                  title: t.title,
   836	                  done: t.status === 'complete' || t.status === 'done',
   837	                  active: state.activeTask?.id === t.id,
   838	                  estimate: t.estimate || undefined,
   839	                });
   840	              }
   841	            }
   842	          }
   843	          if (!usedDbTasks) {
   844	            // File-based fallback: parse slice plan for task entries
   845	            const slicePlanFile = resolveSliceFile(basePath, mid, s.id, 'PLAN');
   846	            if (slicePlanFile) {
   847	              const planContent = readFileCached(slicePlanFile);
   848	              if (planContent) {
   849	                const parsed = parsePlan(planContent);
   850	                for (const t of parsed.tasks) {
   851	                  tasks.push({
   852	                    id: t.id,
   853	                    title: t.title,

   856	                    estimate: t.estimate || undefined,
   857	                  });
   858	                }
   859	              }
   860	            }
   861	          }
   862	        }

     1	import type {
     2	  WorkspaceMilestoneTarget,
     3	  WorkspaceSliceTarget,
     4	  WorkspaceTaskTarget,
     5	} from "./gsd-workspace-store"
     6	
     7	export type ItemStatus = "done" | "in-progress" | "pending"
     8	
     9	export function getMilestoneStatus(
    10	  milestone: WorkspaceMilestoneTarget,
    11	  active: { milestoneId?: string },
    12	): ItemStatus {
    13	  if (milestone.slices.length > 0 && milestone.slices.every((slice) => slice.done)) {
    14	    return "done"
    15	  }
    16	  if (active.milestoneId === milestone.id) {
    17	    return "in-progress"
    18	  }
    19	  return milestone.slices.some((slice) => slice.done) ? "in-progress" : "pending"
    20	}
    21	
    22	export function getSliceStatus(
    23	  milestoneId: string,
    24	  slice: WorkspaceSliceTarget,
    25	  active: { milestoneId?: string; sliceId?: string },
    26	): ItemStatus {
    27	  if (slice.done) return "done"
    28	  if (active.milestoneId === milestoneId && active.sliceId === slice.id) return "in-progress"
    29	  return "pending"
    30	}
    31	
    32	export function getTaskStatus(
    33	  milestoneId: string,
    34	  sliceId: string,
    35	  task: WorkspaceTaskTarget,
    36	  active: { milestoneId?: string; sliceId?: string; taskId?: string },
    37	): ItemStatus {
    38	  if (task.done) return "done"
    39	  if (active.milestoneId === milestoneId && active.sliceId === sliceId && active.taskId === task.id) return "in-progress"
    40	  return "pending"
    41	}

    66	// Extract milestone title from roadmap header without using parsers.
    67	// Falls back to the milestone ID if no title line found.
    68	function titleFromRoadmapHeader(content: string, fallbackId: string): string {
    69	  // Parse the "# M001: Title" header directly
    70	  const match = content.match(/^#\s+M\d+(?:-[a-z0-9]{6})?[^:]*:\s*(.+)/m);
    71	  return match?.[1]?.trim() || fallbackId;
    72	}
    73	
    74	async function indexSlice(basePath: string, milestoneId: string, sliceId: string, fallbackTitle: string, done: boolean, roadmapMeta?: { risk?: RiskLevel; depends?: string[]; demo?: string }): Promise<WorkspaceSliceTarget> {
    75	  const planPath = resolveSliceFile(basePath, milestoneId, sliceId, "PLAN") ?? undefined;
    76	  const summaryPath = resolveSliceFile(basePath, milestoneId, sliceId, "SUMMARY") ?? undefined;
    77	  const uatPath = resolveSliceFile(basePath, milestoneId, sliceId, "UAT") ?? undefined;
    78	  const tasksDir = resolveTasksDir(basePath, milestoneId, sliceId) ?? undefined;
    79	
    80	  const tasks: WorkspaceTaskTarget[] = [];
    81	  let title = fallbackTitle;
    82	
    83	  // Prefer DB for task data, fall back to file parsing when DB has no data
    84	  let usedDb = false;
    85	  if (isDbAvailable()) {
    86	    const dbTasks = getSliceTasks(milestoneId, sliceId);
    87	    if (dbTasks.length > 0) {
    88	      usedDb = true;
    89	      for (const task of dbTasks) {
    90	        title = fallbackTitle; // title comes from slice-level data, not plan
    91	        tasks.push({
    92	          id: task.id,
    93	          title: task.title,
    94	          done: task.status === "complete" || task.status === "done",
    95	          planPath: resolveTaskFile(basePath, milestoneId, sliceId, task.id, "PLAN") ?? undefined,
    96	          summaryPath: resolveTaskFile(basePath, milestoneId, sliceId, task.id, "SUMMARY") ?? undefined,
    97	        });
    98	      }
    99	    }
   100	  }
   101	  if (!usedDb && planPath) {
   102	    // File-based fallback: parse slice plan for task entries
   103	    const planContent = await loadFile(planPath);
   104	    if (planContent) {
   105	      const parsed = parsePlan(planContent);
   106	      for (const task of parsed.tasks) {
   107	        tasks.push({
   108	          id: task.id,
   109	          title: task.title,
   110	          done: task.done,
   111	          planPath: resolveTaskFile(basePath, milestoneId, sliceId, task.id, "PLAN") ?? undefined,
   112	          summaryPath: resolveTaskFile(basePath, milestoneId, sliceId, task.id, "SUMMARY") ?? undefined,
   113	        });
   114	      }
   115	    }
   116	  }
   117	
   118	  return {
   119	    id: sliceId,
   120	    title,
   121	    done,
   122	    planPath,
   123	    summaryPath,
   124	    uatPath,
   125	    tasksDir,
   126	    branch: getSliceBranchName(milestoneId, sliceId, detectWorktreeName(basePath)),
   127	    risk: roadmapMeta?.risk,
   128	    depends: roadmapMeta?.depends,
   129	    demo: roadmapMeta?.demo,
   130	    tasks,
   131	  };
   132	}
   133	
   134	export interface IndexWorkspaceOptions {
   135	  validate?: boolean;
   136	}
   137	
   138	export async function indexWorkspace(basePath: string, opts: IndexWorkspaceOptions = {}): Promise<GSDWorkspaceIndex> {
   139	  const milestoneIds = findMilestoneIds(basePath);
   140	  const milestones: WorkspaceMilestoneTarget[] = [];
   141	
   142	  for (const milestoneId of milestoneIds) {
   143	    const roadmapPath = resolveMilestoneFile(basePath, milestoneId, "ROADMAP") ?? undefined;
   144	    let title = milestoneId;
   145	    const slices: WorkspaceSliceTarget[] = [];
   146	
   147	    if (roadmapPath || isDbAvailable()) {
   148	      // Normalize slices from DB, fall back to file-based parsing when DB has no data
   149	      type NormSlice = { id: string; done: boolean; title: string; risk: string; depends: string[]; demo: string };
   150	      let normSlices: NormSlice[] | null = null;
   151	      if (isDbAvailable()) {
   152	        const dbSlices = getMilestoneSlices(milestoneId);
   153	        if (dbSlices.length > 0) {
   154	          normSlices = dbSlices.map(s => ({ id: s.id, done: s.status === "complete", title: s.title, risk: s.risk || "medium", depends: s.depends, demo: s.demo }));
   155	        }
   156	        // Get title from roadmap header
   157	        if (roadmapPath) {
   158	          const roadmapContent = await loadFile(roadmapPath);
   159	          if (roadmapContent) title = titleFromRoadmapHeader(roadmapContent, milestoneId);
   160	        }
   161	      }
   162	      if (!normSlices && roadmapPath) {
   163	        // File-based fallback: parse roadmap for slice entries
   164	        const roadmapContent = await loadFile(roadmapPath);
   165	        if (roadmapContent) {
   166	          title = titleFromRoadmapHeader(roadmapContent, milestoneId);
   167	          const parsed = parseRoadmap(roadmapContent);
   168	          normSlices = parsed.slices.map(s => ({ id: s.id, done: s.done, title: s.title, risk: s.risk || "medium", depends: s.depends, demo: s.demo || "" }));
   169	        }
   170	      }
   171	      if (!normSlices) normSlices = [];
   172	
   173	      if (normSlices.length > 0) {
   174	        const sliceResults = await Promise.all(
   175	          normSlices.map(async (slice) => {
   176	            return indexSlice(basePath, milestoneId, slice.id, slice.title, slice.done, { risk: slice.risk as RiskLevel, depends: slice.depends, demo: slice.demo });
   177	          }),
   178	        );
   179	
   180	        slices.push(...sliceResults);
   181	      }
   182	    }
   183	
   184	    milestones.push({ id: milestoneId, title, roadmapPath, slices });
   185	  }
   186	
   187	  const state = await deriveState(basePath);
   188	  const active = {
   189	    milestoneId: state.activeMilestone?.id,
   190	    sliceId: state.activeSlice?.id,
   191	    taskId: state.activeTask?.id,
   192	    phase: state.phase,
   193	  };
   194	
   195	  const scopes: WorkspaceScopeTarget[] = [{ scope: "project", label: "project", kind: "project" }];
   196	  for (const milestone of milestones) {
   197	    scopes.push({ scope: milestone.id, label: `${milestone.id}: ${milestone.title}`, kind: "milestone" });
   198	    for (const slice of milestone.slices) {
   199	      scopes.push({ scope: `${milestone.id}/${slice.id}`, label: `${milestone.id}/${slice.id}: ${slice.title}`, kind: "slice" });
   200	      for (const task of slice.tasks) {
   201	        scopes.push({
   202	          scope: `${milestone.id}/${slice.id}/${task.id}`,
   203	          label: `${milestone.id}/${slice.id}/${task.id}: ${task.title}`,
   204	          kind: "task",
   205	        });
   206	      }
   207	    }
   208	  }
   209	
   210	  return { milestones, active, scopes, validationIssues: [] };
   211	}
   212	
   213	export async function listDoctorScopeSuggestions(basePath: string): Promise<Array<{ value: string; label: string }>> {
   214	  const index = await indexWorkspace(basePath);
   215	  const activeSliceScope = index.active.milestoneId && index.active.sliceId
   216	    ? `${index.active.milestoneId}/${index.active.sliceId}`
   217	    : null;
   218	
   219	  const ordered = [...index.scopes].filter(scope => scope.kind !== "project");
   220	  ordered.sort((a, b) => {
   221	    if (activeSliceScope && a.scope === activeSliceScope) return -1;
   222	    if (activeSliceScope && b.scope === activeSliceScope) return 1;
   223	    return a.scope.localeCompare(b.scope);
   224	  });
   225	
   226	  return ordered.map(scope => ({ value: scope.scope, label: scope.label }));
   227	}
   228	
   229	export async function getSuggestedNextCommands(basePath: string): Promise<string[]> {
   230	  const index = await indexWorkspace(basePath);
   231	  const scope = index.active.milestoneId && index.active.sliceId
   232	    ? `${index.active.milestoneId}/${index.active.sliceId}`
   233	    : index.active.milestoneId;
   234	
   235	  const commands = new Set<string>();
   236	  if (index.active.phase === "planning") commands.add("/gsd");
   237	  if (index.active.phase === "executing" || index.active.phase === "summarizing") commands.add("/gsd auto");
   238	  if (scope) commands.add(`/gsd doctor ${scope}`);
   239	  if (scope) commands.add(`/gsd doctor fix ${scope}`);
   240	  commands.add("/gsd status");
   241	  return [...commands];
   242	}

   987	async function loadWorkspaceIndexViaChildProcess(basePath: string, packageRoot: string): Promise<GSDWorkspaceIndex> {
   988	  const deps = getBridgeDeps();
   989	  const checkExists = deps.existsSync ?? existsSync;
   990	  const resolveTsLoader = join(packageRoot, "src", "resources", "extensions", "gsd", "tests", "resolve-ts.mjs");
   991	  const moduleResolution = resolveSubprocessModule(
   992	    packageRoot,
   993	    "resources/extensions/gsd/workspace-index.ts",
   994	    checkExists,
   995	  );
   996	  const workspaceModulePath = moduleResolution.modulePath;
   997	  if (!moduleResolution.useCompiledJs && (!checkExists(resolveTsLoader) || !checkExists(workspaceModulePath))) {
   998	    throw new Error(`workspace index loader not found; checked=${resolveTsLoader},${workspaceModulePath}`);
   999	  }
  1000	  if (moduleResolution.useCompiledJs && !checkExists(workspaceModulePath)) {
  1001	    throw new Error(`workspace index module not found; checked=${workspaceModulePath}`);
  1002	  }
  1003	
  1004	  const script = [
  1005	    'const { pathToFileURL } = await import("node:url");',
  1006	    'const mod = await import(pathToFileURL(process.env.GSD_WORKSPACE_MODULE).href);',
  1007	    'const result = await mod.indexWorkspace(process.env.GSD_WORKSPACE_BASE);',
  1008	    'process.stdout.write(JSON.stringify(result));',
  1009	  ].join(' ');

str_replace_editor str_replace /testbed/src/resources/extensions/gsd/workspace-index.ts   --old_str 'export async function indexWorkspace(basePath: string, opts: IndexWorkspaceOptions = {}): Promise<GSDWorkspaceIndex> {
  const milestoneIds = findMilestoneIds(basePath);
  const milestones: WorkspaceMilestoneTarget[] = [];

  for (const milestoneId of milestoneIds) {
    const roadmapPath = resolveMilestoneFile(basePath, milestoneId, "ROADMAP") ?? undefined;
    let title = milestoneId;
    const slices: WorkspaceSliceTarget[] = [];

    if (roadmapPath || isDbAvailable()) {
      // Normalize slices from DB, fall back to file-based parsing when DB has no data
      type NormSlice = { id: string; done: boolean; title: string; risk: string; depends: string[]; demo: string };
      let normSlices: NormSlice[] | null = null;
      if (isDbAvailable()) {
        const dbSlices = getMilestoneSlices(milestoneId);
        if (dbSlices.length > 0) {
          normSlices = dbSlices.map(s => ({ id: s.id, done: s.status === "complete", title: s.title, risk: s.risk || "medium", depends: s.depends, demo: s.demo }));
        }
        // Get title from roadmap header
        if (roadmapPath) {
          const roadmapContent = await loadFile(roadmapPath);
          if (roadmapContent) title = titleFromRoadmapHeader(roadmapContent, milestoneId);
        }
      }
      if (!normSlices && roadmapPath) {
        // File-based fallback: parse roadmap for slice entries
        const roadmapContent = await loadFile(roadmapPath);
        if (roadmapContent) {
          title = titleFromRoadmapHeader(roadmapContent, milestoneId);
          const parsed = parseRoadmap(roadmapContent);
          normSlices = parsed.slices.map(s => ({ id: s.id, done: s.done, title: s.title, risk: s.risk || "medium", depends: s.depends, demo: s.demo || "" }));
        }
      }
      if (!normSlices) normSlices = [];

      if (normSlices.length > 0) {
        const sliceResults = await Promise.all(
          normSlices.map(async (slice) => {
            return indexSlice(basePath, milestoneId, slice.id, slice.title, slice.done, { risk: slice.risk as RiskLevel, depends: slice.depends, demo: slice.demo });
          }),
        );

        slices.push(...sliceResults);
      }
    }

    milestones.push({ id: milestoneId, title, roadmapPath, slices });
  }

  const state = await deriveState(basePath);
  const active = {
    milestoneId: state.activeMilestone?.id,
    sliceId: state.activeSlice?.id,
    taskId: state.activeTask?.id,
    phase: state.phase,
  };

  const scopes: WorkspaceScopeTarget[] = [{ scope: "project", label: "project", kind: "project" }];
  for (const milestone of milestones) {
    scopes.push({ scope: milestone.id, label: `${milestone.id}: ${milestone.title}`, kind: "milestone" });
    for (const slice of milestone.slices) {
      scopes.push({ scope: `${milestone.id}/${slice.id}`, label: `${milestone.id}/${slice.id}: ${slice.title}`, kind: "slice" });
      for (const task of slice.tasks) {
        scopes.push({
          scope: `${milestone.id}/${slice.id}/${task.id}`,
          label: `${milestone.id}/${slice.id}/${task.id}: ${task.title}`,
          kind: "task",
        });
      }
    }
  }

  return { milestones, active, scopes, validationIssues: [] };
}' --new_str 'export async function indexWorkspace(basePath: string, opts: IndexWorkspaceOptions = {}): Promise<GSDWorkspaceIndex> {
  const milestoneIds = findMilestoneIds(basePath);
  const state = await deriveState(basePath);

  // Build a map of milestone statuses from the authoritative registry
  const registryMap = new Map(state.registry.map(r => [r.id, r]));

  const milestones: WorkspaceMilestoneTarget[] = [];

  for (const milestoneId of milestoneIds) {
    const roadmapPath = resolveMilestoneFile(basePath, milestoneId, "ROADMAP") ?? undefined;
    let title = milestoneId;
    const slices: WorkspaceSliceTarget[] = [];

    if (roadmapPath || isDbAvailable()) {
      // Normalize slices from DB, fall back to file-based parsing when DB has no data
      type NormSlice = { id: string; done: boolean; title: string; risk: string; depends: string[]; demo: string };
      let normSlices: NormSlice[] | null = null;
      if (isDbAvailable()) {
        const dbSlices = getMilestoneSlices(milestoneId);
        if (dbSlices.length > 0) {
          normSlices = dbSlices.map(s => ({ id: s.id, done: s.status === "complete", title: s.title, risk: s.risk || "medium", depends: s.depends, demo: s.demo }));
        }
        // Get title from roadmap header
        if (roadmapPath) {
          const roadmapContent = await loadFile(roadmapPath);
          if (roadmapContent) title = titleFromRoadmapHeader(roadmapContent, milestoneId);
        }
      }
      if (!normSlices && roadmapPath) {
        // File-based fallback: parse roadmap for slice entries
        const roadmapContent = await loadFile(roadmapPath);
        if (roadmapContent) {
          title = titleFromRoadmapHeader(roadmapContent, milestoneId);
          const parsed = parseRoadmap(roadmapContent);
          normSlices = parsed.slices.map(s => ({ id: s.id, done: s.done, title: s.title, risk: s.risk || "medium", depends: s.depends, demo: s.demo || "" }));
        }
      }
      if (!normSlices) normSlices = [];

      if (normSlices.length > 0) {
        const sliceResults = await Promise.all(
          normSlices.map(async (slice) => {
            return indexSlice(basePath, milestoneId, slice.id, slice.title, slice.done, { risk: slice.risk as RiskLevel, depends: slice.depends, demo: slice.demo });
          }),
        );

        slices.push(...sliceResults);
      }
    }

    // Use title from registry when available (more authoritative than roadmap header)
    const registryEntry = registryMap.get(milestoneId);
    if (registryEntry?.title && registryEntry.title !== milestoneId) {
      title = registryEntry.title;
    }

    // Derive authoritative status from the registry
    const status = registryEntry?.status ?? "pending";

    // Derive validation verdict from the milestone VALIDATION file
    let validationVerdict: ValidationVerdict | undefined;
    const validationFile = resolveMilestoneFile(basePath, milestoneId, "VALIDATION");
    if (validationFile) {
      const validationContent = await loadFile(validationFile);
      if (validationContent) {
        const rawVerdict = extractVerdict(validationContent);
        if (rawVerdict === "pass" || rawVerdict === "needs-attention" || rawVerdict === "needs-remediation") {
          validationVerdict = rawVerdict;
        }
      }
    }

    milestones.push({ id: milestoneId, title, roadmapPath, status, validationVerdict, slices });
  }

  const active = {
    milestoneId: state.activeMilestone?.id,
    sliceId: state.activeSlice?.id,
    taskId: state.activeTask?.id,
    phase: state.phase,
  };

  const scopes: WorkspaceScopeTarget[] = [{ scope: "project", label: "project", kind: "project" }];
  for (const milestone of milestones) {
    scopes.push({ scope: milestone.id, label: `${milestone.id}: ${milestone.title}`, kind: "milestone" });
    for (const slice of milestone.slices) {
      scopes.push({ scope: `${milestone.id}/${slice.id}`, label: `${milestone.id}/${slice.id}: ${slice.title}`, kind: "slice" });
      for (const task of slice.tasks) {
        scopes.push({
          scope: `${milestone.id}/${slice.id}/${task.id}`,
          label: `${milestone.id}/${slice.id}/${task.id}: ${task.title}`,
          kind: "task",
        });
      }
    }
  }

  return { milestones, active, scopes, validationIssues: [] };
}'
