   142	export async function indexWorkspace(basePath: string, opts: IndexWorkspaceOptions = {}): Promise<GSDWorkspaceIndex> {
   143	  const milestoneIds = findMilestoneIds(basePath);
   144	  const state = await deriveState(basePath);
   145	
   146	  // Build a map of milestone statuses from the authoritative registry
   147	  const registryMap = new Map(state.registry.map(r => [r.id, r]));
   148	
   149	  const milestones: WorkspaceMilestoneTarget[] = [];
   150	
   151	  for (const milestoneId of milestoneIds) {
   152	    const roadmapPath = resolveMilestoneFile(basePath, milestoneId, "ROADMAP") ?? undefined;
   153	    let title = milestoneId;
   154	    const slices: WorkspaceSliceTarget[] = [];
   155	
   156	    if (roadmapPath || isDbAvailable()) {
   157	      // Normalize slices from DB, fall back to file-based parsing when DB has no data
   158	      type NormSlice = { id: string; done: boolean; title: string; risk: string; depends: string[]; demo: string };
   159	      let normSlices: NormSlice[] | null = null;
   160	      if (isDbAvailable()) {
   161	        const dbSlices = getMilestoneSlices(milestoneId);
   162	        if (dbSlices.length > 0) {
   163	          normSlices = dbSlices.map(s => ({ id: s.id, done: s.status === "complete", title: s.title, risk: s.risk || "medium", depends: s.depends, demo: s.demo }));
   164	        }
   165	        // Get title from roadmap header
   166	        if (roadmapPath) {
   167	          const roadmapContent = await loadFile(roadmapPath);
   168	          if (roadmapContent) title = titleFromRoadmapHeader(roadmapContent, milestoneId);
   169	        }
   170	      }
   171	      if (!normSlices && roadmapPath) {
   172	        // File-based fallback: parse roadmap for slice entries
   173	        const roadmapContent = await loadFile(roadmapPath);
   174	        if (roadmapContent) {
   175	          title = titleFromRoadmapHeader(roadmapContent, milestoneId);
   176	          const parsed = parseRoadmap(roadmapContent);
   177	          normSlices = parsed.slices.map(s => ({ id: s.id, done: s.done, title: s.title, risk: s.risk || "medium", depends: s.depends, demo: s.demo || "" }));
   178	        }
   179	      }
   180	      if (!normSlices) normSlices = [];
   181	
   182	      if (normSlices.length > 0) {
   183	        const sliceResults = await Promise.all(
   184	          normSlices.map(async (slice) => {
   185	            return indexSlice(basePath, milestoneId, slice.id, slice.title, slice.done, { risk: slice.risk as RiskLevel, depends: slice.depends, demo: slice.demo });
   186	          }),
   187	        );
   188	
   189	        slices.push(...sliceResults);
   190	      }
   191	    }
   192	
   193	    // Use title from registry when available (more authoritative than roadmap header)
   194	    const registryEntry = registryMap.get(milestoneId);
   195	    if (registryEntry?.title && registryEntry.title !== milestoneId) {
   196	      title = registryEntry.title;
   197	    }
   198	
   199	    // Derive authoritative status from the registry
   200	    const status = registryEntry?.status ?? "pending";
   201	
   202	    // Derive validation verdict from the milestone VALIDATION file
   203	    let validationVerdict: ValidationVerdict | undefined;
   204	    const validationFile = resolveMilestoneFile(basePath, milestoneId, "VALIDATION");
   205	    if (validationFile) {
   206	      const validationContent = await loadFile(validationFile);
   207	      if (validationContent) {
   208	        const rawVerdict = extractVerdict(validationContent);
   209	        if (rawVerdict === "pass" || rawVerdict === "needs-attention" || rawVerdict === "needs-remediation") {
   210	          validationVerdict = rawVerdict;
   211	        }
   212	      }
   213	    }
   214	
   215	    milestones.push({ id: milestoneId, title, roadmapPath, status, validationVerdict, slices });
   216	  }
   217	
   218	  const active = {
   219	    milestoneId: state.activeMilestone?.id,
   220	    sliceId: state.activeSlice?.id,
   221	    taskId: state.activeTask?.id,
   222	    phase: state.phase,
   223	  };
   224	
   225	  const scopes: WorkspaceScopeTarget[] = [{ scope: "project", label: "project", kind: "project" }];
   226	  for (const milestone of milestones) {
   227	    scopes.push({ scope: milestone.id, label: `${milestone.id}: ${milestone.title}`, kind: "milestone" });
   228	    for (const slice of milestone.slices) {
   229	      scopes.push({ scope: `${milestone.id}/${slice.id}`, label: `${milestone.id}/${slice.id}: ${slice.title}`, kind: "slice" });
   230	      for (const task of slice.tasks) {
   231	        scopes.push({
   232	          scope: `${milestone.id}/${slice.id}/${task.id}`,
   233	          label: `${milestone.id}/${slice.id}/${task.id}: ${task.title}`,
   234	          kind: "task",
   235	        });
   236	      }
   237	    }
   238	  }
   239	
   240	  return { milestones, active, scopes, validationIssues: [] };
   241	}

  WorkspaceMilestoneTarget,

export type ItemStatus = "done" | "in-progress" | "pending"

export function getMilestoneStatus(
  milestone: WorkspaceMilestoneTarget,
  active: { milestoneId?: string },
): ItemStatus {
  if (milestone.slices.length > 0 && milestone.slices.every((slice) => slice.done)) {
    return "done"

  WorkspaceMilestoneTarget,
  WorkspaceSliceTarget,
  WorkspaceTaskTarget,
} from "./gsd-workspace-store"

export type ItemStatus = "done" | "in-progress" | "pending"

export function getMilestoneStatus(
  milestone: WorkspaceMilestoneTarget,
  active: { milestoneId?: string },
): ItemStatus {
  // Prefer authoritative milestone status from the engine/index layer
  if (milestone.status) {
    switch (milestone.status) {
      case "complete":
        return "done"
      case "active":
        return "in-progress"
      case "parked":
      case "pending":
        return "pending"
    }
  }

  // Fallback to slice-based heuristics for backward compatibility
  if (milestone.slices.length > 0 && milestone.slices.every((slice) => slice.done)) {
    return "done"
  }
  if (active.milestoneId === milestone.id) {
    return "in-progress"
  }
  return milestone.slices.some((slice) => slice.done) ? "in-progress" : "pending"
}'

str_replace_editor str_replace /testbed/dist-test/src/resources/extensions/gsd/workspace-index.ts   --old_str 'export async function indexWorkspace(basePath: string, opts: IndexWorkspaceOptions = {}): Promise<GSDWorkspaceIndex> {
  const milestoneIds = findMilestoneIds(basePath);
  const milestones: WorkspaceMilestoneTarget[] = [];

  for (const milestoneId of milestoneIds) {
    const roadmapPath = resolveMilestoneFile(basePath, milestoneId, "ROADMAP") ?? undefined;
    let title = milestoneId;
    const slices: WorkspaceSliceTarget[] = [];

    if (roadmapPath || isDbAvailable()) {
      // Normalize slices from DB, fall back to file-based parsing when DB has no data
      type NormSlice = { id: string; done: boolean; title: string; risk: string; depends: string[]; demo: string };
      let normSlices: NormSlice[] | null = null;
      if (isDbAvailable()) {
        const dbSlices = getMilestoneSlices(milestoneId);
        if (dbSlices.length > 0) {
          normSlices = dbSlices.map(s => ({ id: s.id, done: s.status === "complete", title: s.title, risk: s.risk || "medium", depends: s.depends, demo: s.demo }));
        }
        // Get title from roadmap header
        if (roadmapPath) {
          const roadmapContent = await loadFile(roadmapPath);
          if (roadmapContent) title = titleFromRoadmapHeader(roadmapContent, milestoneId);
        }
      }
      if (!normSlices && roadmapPath) {
        // File-based fallback: parse roadmap for slice entries
        const roadmapContent = await loadFile(roadmapPath);
        if (roadmapContent) {
          title = titleFromRoadmapHeader(roadmapContent, milestoneId);
          const parsed = parseRoadmap(roadmapContent);
          normSlices = parsed.slices.map(s => ({ id: s.id, done: s.done, title: s.title, risk: s.risk || "medium", depends: s.depends, demo: s.demo || "" }));
        }
      }
      if (!normSlices) normSlices = [];

      if (normSlices.length > 0) {
        const sliceResults = await Promise.all(
          normSlices.map(async (slice) => {
            return indexSlice(basePath, milestoneId, slice.id, slice.title, slice.done, { risk: slice.risk as RiskLevel, depends: slice.depends, demo: slice.demo });
          }),
        );

        slices.push(...sliceResults);
      }
    }

    milestones.push({ id: milestoneId, title, roadmapPath, slices });
  }

  const state = await deriveState(basePath);
  const active = {
    milestoneId: state.activeMilestone?.id,
    sliceId: state.activeSlice?.id,
    taskId: state.activeTask?.id,
    phase: state.phase,
  };

  const scopes: WorkspaceScopeTarget[] = [{ scope: "project", label: "project", kind: "project" }];
  for (const milestone of milestones) {
    scopes.push({ scope: milestone.id, label: `${milestone.id}: ${milestone.title}`, kind: "milestone" });
    for (const slice of milestone.slices) {
      scopes.push({ scope: `${milestone.id}/${slice.id}`, label: `${milestone.id}/${slice.id}: ${slice.title}`, kind: "slice" });
      for (const task of slice.tasks) {
        scopes.push({
          scope: `${milestone.id}/${slice.id}/${task.id}`,
          label: `${milestone.id}/${slice.id}/${task.id}: ${task.title}`,
          kind: "task",
        });
      }
    }
  }

  return { milestones, active, scopes, validationIssues: [] };
}' --new_str 'export async function indexWorkspace(basePath: string, opts: IndexWorkspaceOptions = {}): Promise<GSDWorkspaceIndex> {
  const milestoneIds = findMilestoneIds(basePath);
  const state = await deriveState(basePath);

  // Build a map of milestone statuses from the authoritative registry
  const registryMap = new Map(state.registry.map(r => [r.id, r]));

  const milestones: WorkspaceMilestoneTarget[] = [];

  for (const milestoneId of milestoneIds) {
    const roadmapPath = resolveMilestoneFile(basePath, milestoneId, "ROADMAP") ?? undefined;
    let title = milestoneId;
    const slices: WorkspaceSliceTarget[] = [];

    if (roadmapPath || isDbAvailable()) {
      // Normalize slices from DB, fall back to file-based parsing when DB has no data
      type NormSlice = { id: string; done: boolean; title: string; risk: string; depends: string[]; demo: string };
      let normSlices: NormSlice[] | null = null;
      if (isDbAvailable()) {
        const dbSlices = getMilestoneSlices(milestoneId);
        if (dbSlices.length > 0) {
          normSlices = dbSlices.map(s => ({ id: s.id, done: s.status === "complete", title: s.title, risk: s.risk || "medium", depends: s.depends, demo: s.demo }));
        }
        // Get title from roadmap header
        if (roadmapPath) {
          const roadmapContent = await loadFile(roadmapPath);
          if (roadmapContent) title = titleFromRoadmapHeader(roadmapContent, milestoneId);
        }
      }
      if (!normSlices && roadmapPath) {
        // File-based fallback: parse roadmap for slice entries
        const roadmapContent = await loadFile(roadmapPath);
        if (roadmapContent) {
          title = titleFromRoadmapHeader(roadmapContent, milestoneId);
          const parsed = parseRoadmap(roadmapContent);
          normSlices = parsed.slices.map(s => ({ id: s.id, done: s.done, title: s.title, risk: s.risk || "medium", depends: s.depends, demo: s.demo || "" }));
        }
      }
      if (!normSlices) normSlices = [];

      if (normSlices.length > 0) {
        const sliceResults = await Promise.all(
          normSlices.map(async (slice) => {
            return indexSlice(basePath, milestoneId, slice.id, slice.title, slice.done, { risk: slice.risk as RiskLevel, depends: slice.depends, demo: slice.demo });
          }),
        );

        slices.push(...sliceResults);
      }

    // Use title from registry when available (more authoritative than roadmap header)
    const registryEntry = registryMap.get(milestoneId);
    if (registryEntry?.title && registryEntry.title !== milestoneId) {
      title = registryEntry.title;
    }

    // Derive authoritative status from the registry
    const status = registryEntry?.status ?? "pending";

    // Derive validation verdict from the milestone VALIDATION file
    let validationVerdict: ValidationVerdict | undefined;
    const validationFile = resolveMilestoneFile(basePath, milestoneId, "VALIDATION");
    if (validationFile) {
      const validationContent = await loadFile(validationFile);
      if (validationContent) {
        const rawVerdict = extractVerdict(validationContent);
        if (rawVerdict === "pass" || rawVerdict === "needs-attention" || rawVerdict === "needs-remediation") {
          validationVerdict = rawVerdict;
        }
      }
    }

    milestones.push({ id: milestoneId, title, roadmapPath, status, validationVerdict, slices });
  }

  const active = {
    milestoneId: state.activeMilestone?.id,
    sliceId: state.activeSlice?.id,
    taskId: state.activeTask?.id,
    phase: state.phase,
  };

  const scopes: WorkspaceScopeTarget[] = [{ scope: "project", label: "project", kind: "project" }];
  for (const milestone of milestones) {
    scopes.push({ scope: milestone.id, label: `${milestone.id}: ${milestone.title}`, kind: "milestone" });
    for (const slice of milestone.slices) {
      scopes.push({ scope: `${milestone.id}/${slice.id}`, label: `${milestone.id}/${slice.id}: ${slice.title}`, kind: "slice" });
      for (const task of slice.tasks) {
        scopes.push({
          scope: `${milestone.id}/${slice.id}/${task.id}`,
          label: `${milestone.id}/${slice.id}/${task.id}: ${task.title}`,
          kind: "task",
        });
      }
    }
  }

  return { milestones, active, scopes, validationIssues: [] };

  WorkspaceMilestoneTarget,
  WorkspaceSliceTarget,
  WorkspaceTaskTarget,
} from "./gsd-workspace-store"

export type ItemStatus = "done" | "in-progress" | "pending"

export function getMilestoneStatus(
  milestone: WorkspaceMilestoneTarget,
  active: { milestoneId?: string },
): ItemStatus {
  // Prefer authoritative milestone status from the engine/index layer
  if (milestone.status) {
    switch (milestone.status) {
      case "complete":
        return "done"
      case "active":
        return "in-progress"
      case "parked":
      case "pending":
        return "pending"
    }
  }

  // Fallback to slice-based heuristics for backward compatibility
  if (milestone.slices.length > 0 && milestone.slices.every((slice) => slice.done)) {
    return "done"
  }
  if (active.milestoneId === milestone.id) {
    return "in-progress"
  }
  return milestone.slices.some((slice) => slice.done) ? "in-progress" : "pending"
}'

Here's the result of running `cat -n` on /testbed/web/lib/workspace-status.ts:
     1	import type {
     2	  WorkspaceMilestoneTarget,
     3	  WorkspaceSliceTarget,
     4	  WorkspaceTaskTarget,
     5	} from "./gsd-workspace-store"
     6	
     7	export type ItemStatus = "done" | "in-progress" | "pending"
     8	
     9	export function getMilestoneStatus(
    10	  milestone: WorkspaceMilestoneTarget,
    11	  active: { milestoneId?: string },
    12	): ItemStatus {
    13	  // Prefer authoritative milestone status from the engine/index layer
    14	  if (milestone.status) {
    15	    switch (milestone.status) {
    16	      case "complete":
    17	        return "done"
    18	      case "active":
    19	        return "in-progress"
    20	      case "parked":
    21	      case "pending":
    22	        return "pending"
    23	    }
    24	  }
    25	
    26	  // Fallback to slice-based heuristics for backward compatibility
    27	  if (milestone.slices.length > 0 && milestone.slices.every((slice) => slice.done)) {
    28	    return "done"
    29	  }
    30	  if (active.milestoneId === milestone.id) {
    31	    return "in-progress"
    32	  }
    33	  return milestone.slices.some((slice) => slice.done) ? "in-progress" : "pending"
    34	}
    35	
    36	export function getSliceStatus(
    37	  milestoneId: string,
    38	  slice: WorkspaceSliceTarget,
    39	  active: { milestoneId?: string; sliceId?: string },
    40	): ItemStatus {
    41	  if (slice.done) return "done"
    42	  if (active.milestoneId === milestoneId && active.sliceId === slice.id) return "in-progress"
    43	  return "pending"
    44	}
    45	
    46	export function getTaskStatus(
    47	  milestoneId: string,
    48	  sliceId: string,
    49	  task: WorkspaceTaskTarget,
    50	  active: { milestoneId?: string; sliceId?: string; taskId?: string },
    51	): ItemStatus {
    52	  if (task.done) return "done"
    53	  if (active.milestoneId === milestoneId && active.sliceId === sliceId && active.taskId === task.id) return "in-progress"
    54	  return "pending"

    70	// Extract milestone title from roadmap header without using parsers.
    71	// Falls back to the milestone ID if no title line found.
    72	function titleFromRoadmapHeader(content: string, fallbackId: string): string {
    73	  // Parse the "# M001: Title" header directly
    74	  const match = content.match(/^#\s+M\d+(?:-[a-z0-9]{6})?[^:]*:\s*(.+)/m);
    75	  return match?.[1]?.trim() || fallbackId;
    76	}
    77	
    78	async function indexSlice(basePath: string, milestoneId: string, sliceId: string, fallbackTitle: string, done: boolean, roadmapMeta?: { risk?: RiskLevel; depends?: string[]; demo?: string }): Promise<WorkspaceSliceTarget> {
    79	  const planPath = resolveSliceFile(basePath, milestoneId, sliceId, "PLAN") ?? undefined;
    80	  const summaryPath = resolveSliceFile(basePath, milestoneId, sliceId, "SUMMARY") ?? undefined;
    81	  const uatPath = resolveSliceFile(basePath, milestoneId, sliceId, "UAT") ?? undefined;
    82	  const tasksDir = resolveTasksDir(basePath, milestoneId, sliceId) ?? undefined;
    83	
    84	  const tasks: WorkspaceTaskTarget[] = [];
    85	  let title = fallbackTitle;
    86	
    87	  // Prefer DB for task data, fall back to file parsing when DB has no data
    88	  let usedDb = false;
    89	  if (isDbAvailable()) {
    90	    const dbTasks = getSliceTasks(milestoneId, sliceId);
    91	    if (dbTasks.length > 0) {
    92	      usedDb = true;
    93	      for (const task of dbTasks) {
    94	        title = fallbackTitle; // title comes from slice-level data, not plan
    95	        tasks.push({
    96	          id: task.id,
    97	          title: task.title,
    98	          done: task.status === "complete" || task.status === "done",
    99	          planPath: resolveTaskFile(basePath, milestoneId, sliceId, task.id, "PLAN") ?? undefined,
   100	          summaryPath: resolveTaskFile(basePath, milestoneId, sliceId, task.id, "SUMMARY") ?? undefined,
   101	        });
   102	      }
   103	    }
   104	  }
   105	  if (!usedDb && planPath) {
   106	    // File-based fallback: parse slice plan for task entries
   107	    const planContent = await loadFile(planPath);
   108	    if (planContent) {
   109	      const parsed = parsePlan(planContent);
   110	      for (const task of parsed.tasks) {
   111	        tasks.push({
   112	          id: task.id,
   113	          title: task.title,
   114	          done: task.done,
   115	          planPath: resolveTaskFile(basePath, milestoneId, sliceId, task.id, "PLAN") ?? undefined,
   116	          summaryPath: resolveTaskFile(basePath, milestoneId, sliceId, task.id, "SUMMARY") ?? undefined,
   117	        });
   118	      }
   119	    }
   120	  }
   121	
   122	  return {
   123	    id: sliceId,
   124	    title,
   125	    done,
   126	    planPath,
   127	    summaryPath,
   128	    uatPath,
   129	    tasksDir,
   130	    branch: getSliceBranchName(milestoneId, sliceId, detectWorktreeName(basePath)),
   131	    risk: roadmapMeta?.risk,
   132	    depends: roadmapMeta?.depends,
   133	    demo: roadmapMeta?.demo,
   134	    tasks,
   135	  };
   136	}

   138	export interface IndexWorkspaceOptions {
   139	  validate?: boolean;
   140	}
   141	
   142	export async function indexWorkspace(basePath: string, opts: IndexWorkspaceOptions = {}): Promise<GSDWorkspaceIndex> {
   143	  const milestoneIds = findMilestoneIds(basePath);
   144	  const state = await deriveState(basePath);
   145	
   146	  // Build a map of milestone statuses from the authoritative registry
   147	  const registryMap = new Map(state.registry.map(r => [r.id, r]));
   148	
   149	  const milestones: WorkspaceMilestoneTarget[] = [];
   150	
   151	  for (const milestoneId of milestoneIds) {
   152	    const roadmapPath = resolveMilestoneFile(basePath, milestoneId, "ROADMAP") ?? undefined;
   153	    let title = milestoneId;
   154	    const slices: WorkspaceSliceTarget[] = [];
   155	
   156	    if (roadmapPath || isDbAvailable()) {
   157	      // Normalize slices from DB, fall back to file-based parsing when DB has no data
   158	      type NormSlice = { id: string; done: boolean; title: string; risk: string; depends: string[]; demo: string };
   159	      let normSlices: NormSlice[] | null = null;
   160	      if (isDbAvailable()) {
   161	        const dbSlices = getMilestoneSlices(milestoneId);
   162	        if (dbSlices.length > 0) {
   163	          normSlices = dbSlices.map(s => ({ id: s.id, done: s.status === "complete", title: s.title, risk: s.risk || "medium", depends: s.depends, demo: s.demo }));
   164	        }
   165	        // Get title from roadmap header
   166	        if (roadmapPath) {
   167	          const roadmapContent = await loadFile(roadmapPath);
   168	          if (roadmapContent) title = titleFromRoadmapHeader(roadmapContent, milestoneId);
   169	        }
   170	      }
   171	      if (!normSlices && roadmapPath) {
   172	        // File-based fallback: parse roadmap for slice entries
   173	        const roadmapContent = await loadFile(roadmapPath);
   174	        if (roadmapContent) {
   175	          title = titleFromRoadmapHeader(roadmapContent, milestoneId);
   176	          const parsed = parseRoadmap(roadmapContent);
   177	          normSlices = parsed.slices.map(s => ({ id: s.id, done: s.done, title: s.title, risk: s.risk || "medium", depends: s.depends, demo: s.demo || "" }));
   178	        }
   179	      }
   180	      if (!normSlices) normSlices = [];
   181	
   182	      if (normSlices.length > 0) {
   183	        const sliceResults = await Promise.all(
   184	          normSlices.map(async (slice) => {
   185	            return indexSlice(basePath, milestoneId, slice.id, slice.title, slice.done, { risk: slice.risk as RiskLevel, depends: slice.depends, demo: slice.demo });
   186	          }),
   187	        );
   188	
   189	        slices.push(...sliceResults);
   190	      }
   191	    }
   192	
   193	    // Use title from registry when available (more authoritative than roadmap header)
   194	    const registryEntry = registryMap.get(milestoneId);
   195	    if (registryEntry?.title && registryEntry.title !== milestoneId) {
   196	      title = registryEntry.title;
   197	    }
   198	
   199	    // Derive authoritative status from the registry
   200	    const status = registryEntry?.status ?? "pending";
   201	
   202	    // Derive validation verdict from the milestone VALIDATION file
   203	    let validationVerdict: ValidationVerdict | undefined;
   204	    const validationFile = resolveMilestoneFile(basePath, milestoneId, "VALIDATION");
   205	    if (validationFile) {
   206	      const validationContent = await loadFile(validationFile);
   207	      if (validationContent) {
   208	        const rawVerdict = extractVerdict(validationContent);
   209	        if (rawVerdict === "pass" || rawVerdict === "needs-attention" || rawVerdict === "needs-remediation") {
   210	          validationVerdict = rawVerdict;
   211	        }
   212	      }
   213	    }
   214	
   215	    milestones.push({ id: milestoneId, title, roadmapPath, status, validationVerdict, slices });
   216	  }
   217	
   218	  const active = {
   219	    milestoneId: state.activeMilestone?.id,
   220	    sliceId: state.activeSlice?.id,
   221	    taskId: state.activeTask?.id,
   222	    phase: state.phase,
   223	  };
   224	
   225	  const scopes: WorkspaceScopeTarget[] = [{ scope: "project", label: "project", kind: "project" }];
   226	  for (const milestone of milestones) {
   227	    scopes.push({ scope: milestone.id, label: `${milestone.id}: ${milestone.title}`, kind: "milestone" });
   228	    for (const slice of milestone.slices) {
   229	      scopes.push({ scope: `${milestone.id}/${slice.id}`, label: `${milestone.id}/${slice.id}: ${slice.title}`, kind: "slice" });
   230	      for (const task of slice.tasks) {
   231	        scopes.push({
   232	          scope: `${milestone.id}/${slice.id}/${task.id}`,
   233	          label: `${milestone.id}/${slice.id}/${task.id}: ${task.title}`,
   234	          kind: "task",
   235	        });
   236	      }
   237	    }
   238	  }
   239	
   240	  return { milestones, active, scopes, validationIssues: [] };
   241	}
   242	
   243	export async function listDoctorScopeSuggestions(basePath: string): Promise<Array<{ value: string; label: string }>> {
   244	  const index = await indexWorkspace(basePath);
   245	  const activeSliceScope = index.active.milestoneId && index.active.sliceId
   246	    ? `${index.active.milestoneId}/${index.active.sliceId}`
   247	    : null;
   248	
   249	  const ordered = [...index.scopes].filter(scope => scope.kind !== "project");
   250	  ordered.sort((a, b) => {
   251	    if (activeSliceScope && a.scope === activeSliceScope) return -1;
   252	    if (activeSliceScope && b.scope === activeSliceScope) return 1;
   253	    return a.scope.localeCompare(b.scope);
   254	  });
   255	
   256	  return ordered.map(scope => ({ value: scope.scope, label: scope.label }));
   257	}
   258	
   259	export async function getSuggestedNextCommands(basePath: string): Promise<string[]> {
   260	  const index = await indexWorkspace(basePath);
   261	  const scope = index.active.milestoneId && index.active.sliceId
   262	    ? `${index.active.milestoneId}/${index.active.sliceId}`
   263	    : index.active.milestoneId;
   264	
   265	  const commands = new Set<string>();
   266	  if (index.active.phase === "planning") commands.add("/gsd");
   267	  if (index.active.phase === "executing" || index.active.phase === "summarizing") commands.add("/gsd auto");
   268	  if (scope) commands.add(`/gsd doctor ${scope}`);
   269	  if (scope) commands.add(`/gsd doctor fix ${scope}`);
   270	  commands.add("/gsd status");
   271	  return [...commands];
   272	}

@@ -10,6 +10,20 @@ export function getMilestoneStatus(
   milestone: WorkspaceMilestoneTarget,
   active: { milestoneId?: string },
 ): ItemStatus {
+  // Prefer authoritative milestone status from the engine/index layer
+  if (milestone.status) {
+    switch (milestone.status) {
+      case "complete":
+        return "done"
+      case "active":
+        return "in-progress"
+      case "parked":
+      case "pending":
+        return "pending"
+    }
+  }
+
+  // Fallback to slice-based heuristics for backward compatibility
   if (milestone.slices.length > 0 && milestone.slices.every((slice) => slice.done)) {
     return "done"
   }

@@ -10,6 +10,20 @@ export function getMilestoneStatus(
   milestone: WorkspaceMilestoneTarget,
   active: { milestoneId?: string },
 ): ItemStatus {
+  // Prefer authoritative milestone status from the engine/index layer
+  if (milestone.status) {
+    switch (milestone.status) {
+      case "complete":
+        return "done"
+      case "active":
+        return "in-progress"
+      case "parked":
+      case "pending":
+        return "pending"
+    }
+  }
+
+  // Fallback to slice-based heuristics for backward compatibility
   if (milestone.slices.length > 0 && milestone.slices.every((slice) => slice.done)) {
     return "done"
   }
